4. Disvāna yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato santike imā gāthayo abhāsi:|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
balivaddā catuddasa||
ajjasaṭṭhiɱ na dissanti||
tenāyaɱ samaṇo sukhī.|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
tilā khettasmiɱ pāpikā||
ekapaṇṇā dvipannā ca||
tenāyam samaṇo sukhī.|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
tuccha-kotthasmiɱ musikā||
ussoḷhikaya naccanti||
tenāyaɱ samaṇo sukhī.|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
santhāro sattamāsiko||
uppāṭakehi saɱchanno||
tenāyaɱ samaṇo sukhī.|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
vidhavā sattadhītaro||
ekaputtā dviputtā cā||
tenāyaɱ samaṇo sukhī.|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
piŋgalā tilakā hatā||
sottam pādena bodheti||
tenāyaɱ samaṇo sukhī.|| ||

Na hi nūn-imassa samaṇassa||
paccūsamhi iṇāyikā||
detha dethā ti codenti||
tenāyaɱ samaṇo sukhī ti.|| ||

5. Na hi mayham brāhmaṇa||
balivaddā catuddasa||
ajjasaṭṭhiɱ na dissanti||
tenāhaɱ brāhmaṇa sukhī.|| ||

[page 171]

Na hi mayham brāhmaṇa||
tilā khettasmiɱ pāpikā||
ekapaṇṇā dvipaṇṇā ca||
teṇāhaɱ brāhmaṇa sukhī.|| ||

Na hi mayham brāhmaṇa||
tucchā-koṭṭhasmiɱ musikā||
ussoḷhikāya naccanti||
tenāhaɱ brāhmaṇa sukhī.|| ||

Na hi mayhaɱ brāhmaṇa||
santhāro sattamāsiko||
uppāṭakehi saɱchanno||
tenāham brāhmaṇa sukhī.|| ||

Na hi mayham brāhmaṇa||
vidhavā sattadhītaro||
ekaputtā driputtā ca||
tenāhaɱ brāhmaṇa sukhī.|| ||

Na hi mayhaɱ brāhmaṇa||
piŋgalā tilakā hatā||
sottam pādena bodheti||
tenāhaɱ brāhmaṇa sukhī.|| ||

Na hi mayhaɱ brāhmaṇa||
paccūsamhi iṇāyikā||
detha dethāti codenti||
tenāhaɱ brāhmaṇa sukhī ti.|| ||

6. Evam vutte bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama abhikkantam bho Gotama||
seyyathāpi bho Gotama nikujjitam va ukkujjeyya paṭicchannaɱ vā vivareyya||
mūḷhassa vā maggam ācikkheyya||
andhakāre telapajjotaɱ dhāreyya cakkhumanto rupāni dakkhinti||
evam evam bhotā Gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito||
esāhaɱ Bhagavantam saraṇaɱ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaŋghañca||
Labheyyāhaɱ bhoto Gotamassa santike pabbajjaɱ labheyyam upasampadan ti.|| ||

7. Alattha kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo Bhagavato santike pabbajjam alattha upasampadaɱ.|| ||

8. Acirūpasampanno panāyasmā bharadvājo eko vūpakaṭṭho appamatto ātāpī pahitatto viharanto na cirass-eva yassattāya kulaputtā sammadeva agārasmā anagāriyaɱ pabbajanti||
tad anuttaraɱ brahmacariyapariyosānaɱ diṭṭheva dhamme sayam abhiññā sacchikatvā upasampajja vihāsi||
khīnā jāti vusitaɱ brahmacariyaɱ kataɱ karaṇīyaɱ nāparam itthattāyā ti abbhaññāsi.|| ||

9. Aññataro ca panāyasmā bhāradvājo arahatam ahosī ti.|| ||

Arahanta-vaggo pathamo.|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Dhanañjānī ca Akkosaɱ||
Asurinda Bilaŋgikaɱ||
Ahiɱsakaɱ Jaṭā c-eva||
Suddhikaɱ c-eva Aggikā||
Sundarikaɱ Bahudhīti||
yena ca te dasā ti.|| ||

[page 172]

 

 

Chapter II: Upāsaka Vaggo

1. Kasi

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Magadhesu viharati Dakkhiṇāgirismiɱ Ekanālāyam brāhmaṇa-gāme.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena kasi-bhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa pañcamattāni naŋgalasatāni payuttāni honti vappakāle.|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena kasi-bhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa kammanto ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Tena kho pana samayena kasi-bhāradvājassa brāhmaṇassa parivesanā vattati.|| ||

5. Atha kho Bhagavā yena parivesanā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā eka-m-antam aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

6. Addasā kho kasi-bharadvājo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam piṇḍāya ṭhitaɱ||
disvāna Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Ahaɱ kho samaṇa kasāmi ca vapāmi ca||
kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmi|| ||

Tvam pi samaṇa kasassu ca vapassu ca||
kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjassī ti.|| ||

7. Aham pi kho brāhmaṇa kasāmi ca vapāmi ca||
kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī ti.|| ||

8. Na kho mayam passāma bhoto Gotamassa yugaɱ vā vā naŋgalaɱ vā phālaɱ vā pācanam vā balivadde vā||
atha ca pana bhavaɱ Gotamo evam āha|| ||

Aham pi kho brāhmaṇa kasāmi ca vapāmi ca||
kasitvā ca vapitvā ca bhuñjāmī ti.|| ||

9. Atha kho kasi-bhāradvājo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Kassako paṭijānāsi||
na ca passāmi te kasiɱ||
kassako pucchito brūhi||
kathaɱ jānemu taɱ kasin ti.|| ||

10. Saddhā bījaɱ tapo vuṭṭhi||
paññā me yuganaŋgalaɱ||
hirī isā mano yottaɱ||
sati me phāla-pācanaɱ.|| ||

Kāyagutto vacīgutto||
āhāre udare yato||
saccaɱ karomi niddānaɱ||
soraccam me pamocanaɱ.|| ||

[page 173]

Viriyam me dhuradhorayhaɱ||
yogakkhemādhivāhanaɱ||
gacchati anivattantaɱ||
yattha gantvā na socati.|| ||

Evam esā kasī kaṭṭhā||
sā hoti amatapphalā||
etaɱ kasiɱ kasitvāna||
sabbadukkhā pamuccatī ti.|| ||

11. Bhuñjatu bhavaɱ Gotamo kassako bhavaɱ Gotamo||
yaɱ hi Gotamo amatapphalam pi kasiɱ kasatī ti.|| ||

12. Gāthābhigītam me abhojanīyaɱ||
sampassataɱ brāhmaṇa n-esa dhammo||
gāthābhigītaɱ panudanti buddhā||
dhamme sati brāhmaṇa vuttir esā.|| ||

Aññena ce kevalinaɱ mahesiɱ||
khīṇāsavaɱ kukkuccavūpasantaɱ||
annena pānena upaṭṭhahassu||
khettañhi taɱ puññapekkhassa hotī ti|| ||

Evaɱ vutte kasi-bhāradvājo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama||
seyyathāpi bho Gotama nikkujjitaɱ vā ukkujjeyya paṭicchannaɱ vā vivareyya mūḷhassa vā maggaɱ ācikkheyya andhakāre vā telapajjotaɱ dhāreyya cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhinti||
evam evam bho Gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito||
esāhaɱ bhagavantaɱ Gotamaɱ saraṇaɱ gacchāmi dhammañca bhikkhusaŋghañca||
upāsakaɱ maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dharetu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

2. Udayo

1. Sāvatthi nidānam.|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Udayassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaɱ tenupasaŋkami.|| ||

3. Atha kho Udayo brāhmaṇo Bhagavato pattam odanena pūresi.|| ||

4. Dutiyam pi kho Bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Udayassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaɱ ten-upasaŋkami||
pa||
5. Tatiyam pi kho Udayo brāhmaṇo Bhagavato pattam

[page 174]

odanena pūretvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Pakaṭṭhako yaɱ samaṇo Gotamo punappunam āgacchatī ti.|| ||

Punappunam ceva vapanti bījaɱ||
punappunaɱ vassati devarājā||
punappunam khettam kasanti kassakā||
punappunam aññam upeti raṭṭhaɱ.|| ||

Punappunaɱ yācakā yācayanti||
punappunam dānapatī dadanti||
punappunam dānapatī daditvā||
punappunam saggam upeti ṭhānaɱ.|| ||

Punappunaɱ khīranikā duhanti||
punappunaɱ vaccho upeti mātaraɱ||
punappunaɱ kilamati phandati ca||
punappunaɱ gabbham upeti mando.|| ||

Punappunaɱ jāyati miyyati ca||
punappunaɱ sīvathikaɱ haranti||
maggañca laddhā apunabbhavāya||
na punappunam jāyati bhūripañño ti.|| ||

7. Evam vutte Udayo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
Upāsakam maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

3. Devahito

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā vātehi ābādhiko hoti||
āyasmā ca Upavāno Bhagavato upaṭṭhāko hoti.|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā āyasmantam Upavānam āmantesi.|| ||

Iŋgha me tvaɱ Upavāna uṇhodakaɱ jānāhī ti.|| ||

4. Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā Upavāno Bhagavato paṭissutvā nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Devahitassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaɱ ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā tuṇhībhūto eka-m-antam aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

5. Addasā kho Devahito brāhmaṇo āyasmantam Upavānam tuṇhībhutam eka-m-antam ṭhitaɱ||
disvāna āyasmantam Upavānaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

[page 175]

Tuṇhībhūto bhavaɱ tiṭṭhaɱ||
muṇḍo saŋghāṭipāruto||
kiɱ patthayāno kim esaɱ||
kiɱ nu yācitum āgato ti.|| ||

6. Arahaɱ Sugato loke||
vātehābadhiko muni||
sace uṇhodakam atthi||
munino dehi brāhmaṇa||
pūjito pūjaneyyānaɱ||
sakkareyyānam sakkato||
apacito apaceyyānaɱ||
tassa icchāmi hātave ti.|| ||

7. Atha kho Devahito brāhmaṇo uṇhodakassa kājam purisena gāhāpetvā phāṇitassa ca puṭam āyasmato Upavānassa pādāsi.|| ||

8. Atha kho āyasmā Upavāno yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam uṇhodakena nahāpetvā uṇhodakena phāṇitam āloḷetvā Bhagavato pādāsi.|| ||

9. Atha kho Bhagavato so ābādho paṭippassambhi.|| ||

10. Atha kho Devahito brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhim sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi.|| ||

11. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho Devahito brāhmaṇo Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Kattha dajjā deyyadhammam||
kattha dinnaɱ mahapphalaɱ||
kathaɱ hi yajamānassa||
katham ijjhati dakkhiṇā ti.|| ||

12. Pubbe nivāsam yo vedi||
saggāpāyañca passati||
atho jātikkhayaɱ patto||
abhiññāvosito muni.|| ||

Ettha dajjā deyyadhammam||
ettha dinnam mahapphalaɱ||
evaɱ hi yajamānassa||
evam ijjhati dakkhiṇā ti.|| ||

13. Evaɱ vutte Devahito brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

4. Mahāsāla (or Lūkhapāpuraṇa)

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Atha kho aññataro brāhmaṇa-mahāsālo lūkho lūkhapā-

[page 176]

puraṇo yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyam vītisāretvā eka-m-antam nisīdi|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho taɱ brāhmaṇa-mahāsālaɱ Bhagavā etad avocā|| ||

Kin nu tvaɱ brāhmaṇa lūkho lūkhapāpuraṇo ti.|| ||

4. Idha me bho Gotama cattaro puttā||
te maɱ dārehi sampuccha gharā nikkhamentī ti.|| ||

5. Tena hi tvaɱ brāhmaṇa imā gāthāyo pariyāpuṇitvā sabhāyaɱ mahājanakāye sannipatite puttesu ca sannisinnesu bhāsassu.|| ||

Yehi jātehi nandissaɱ||
yesañ ca bhavam icchisaɱ||
te maɱ dārehi sampuccha||
sā va vārenti sūkaraɱ.|| ||

Asantā kira maɱ jammā||
tāta tātā ti bhāsare||
rakkhasā puttarūpena||
te jahanti vayogataɱ.|| ||

Asso va jiṇṇo nibbhogo||
khādanā apanīyati||
bālakānam pitā thero||
parāgāresu bhikkhati.|| ||

Daṇḍo va kira me seyyo||
yañ ce puttā anassavā||
caṇḍam pi gonam vāreti||
atho caṇḍam pi kukkuraɱ.|| ||

Andhakāre pure hoti||
gambhīre gādham edhati||
daṇḍassa ānubhāvena||
khalitvā paṭitiṭṭhatī ti.|| ||

6. Atha kho so brāhmaṇa-mahāsālo Bhagavato santike imā gāthāyo pariyāpuṇitvā sabhāyaɱ mahājanakāye sannipatite puttesu ca sannisinnesu abhāsi:|| ||

Yehi jātehi nandissam||
yesañ ca bhavam icchisaɱ||
te maɱ dārehi sampuccha||
sā va vārenti sūkaram.|| ||

Asantā kira maɱ jammā||
tāta tātā ti bhāsare||
rakkhasā puttarūpena||
te jahanti vayogataɱ.|| ||

Asso va jiṇṇo nibbhogo||
khādanā apanīyati||
bālakānam pitā thero||
parāgāresu bhikkhati.|| ||

Daṇḍo va kira me seyyo||
yañ ce puttā anassavā||
caṇḍam pi goṇaɱ vāreti||
atho caṇḍam pi kukkuraɱ.|| ||

Andhakāre pure hoti||
gambhīre gādham edhati||
daṇḍassa ānubhāvena||
khalitvā patitiṭṭhatī ti.|| ||

[page 177]

7. Atha kho naɱ brāhmaṇa-mahāsālaɱ puttā gharaɱ netvā nahāpetvā paccekaɱ dussayugena acchādesuɱ.|| ||

8. Atha kho so brāhmaṇa-mahāsālo ekaɱ dussayugam ādāya yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi.|| ||

9. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho brāhmaṇa-mahāsālo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Mayam bho Gotama brāhmaṇā nāma ācariyassa ācariyadhanam pariyesāma||
patiggaṇhatu me bhavaɱ Gotamo ācariyadhanan ti.|| ||

10. Paṭiggahesi Bhagavā anukampam upādāya.|| ||

11. Atha kho so brāhmaṇa-mahāsālo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ mam bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

5. Mānatthaddo

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Mānatthaddho nāma brāhmaṇo Sāvatthiyaɱ pativasati||
so n'eva mātaram abhivādeti||
na pitaram abhivādeti||
na ācariyam abhivādeti||
na jeṭṭhabhātaram abhivādeti.|| ||

3. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā mahatiya parisāya parivuto dhammaɱ desesi.|| ||

4. Atha kho Mānatthaddhassa brāhmaṇassa etad ahosi.|| ||

Ayaɱ kho samaṇo Gotamo mahatiyā parisāya parivuto dhammaɱ deseti||
yaɱ nūnāham yena samaṇo Gotamo tenupasaŋkameyyaɱ||
sace maɱ samaṇo Gotamo ālapissati aham pi tam ālapissāmi||
no ce maɱ samaṇo Gotamo ālapissati aham pi taɱ nālapissāmī ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho Mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā tuṇhībhūto eka-m-antam aṭṭhāsi.|| ||

6. Atha kho Bhagavā taɱ nālapi.|| ||

7. Atha kho Mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo||
nāyaɱ samaṇo Gotamo kiñci jānātī ti||
tato puna-nivattitu-kāmo ahosi.|| ||

[page 178]

8. Atha kho Bhagavā Mānatthaddhassa brāhmaṇassa cetasā ceto-parivitakkam aññāya Mānatthaddhaɱ brāhmaṇaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Na mānaɱ brāhmaṇa sādhu||
atthi kassīdha brāhmaṇa||
yena atthena āgacchi||
tam evam anubrūhaye ti.|| ||

9. Atha kho Mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo||
cittam me samaṇo Gotamo jānātī ti||
tatth-eva Bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipativā Bhagavato pādāni mukhena ca paricumbati pāṇīhi ca parisambāhati nāmañ ca sāveti Mānatthaddhāham bho Gotama Mānatthaddhāham bho Gotamā ti.|| ||

10. Atha kho sā parisā abbhutacittajātā ahosi.|| ||

Acchariyaɱ vata bho abbhutam vata bho||
ayaɱ hi Mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo n'eva mātaram abhivādeti||
na pitaram abhivādeti||
na ācariyam abhivādeti||
na jeṭṭhabhātaram abhivādeti||
atha ca pana samaṇe Gotame evarūpaɱ paramaɱ nipaccākāraɱ karotī ti.|| ||

11. Atha kho Bhagavā Mānatthaddhaɱ brāhmaṇaɱ etad avoca:|| ||

Alaɱ brāhmaṇa uṭṭhehi sake āsane nisīda yato te mayi cittaɱ pasannan ti.|| ||

12. Atha kho Mānatthaddho brāhmaṇo sake āsane nisīditvā Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Kesu na mānaɱ kayirātha||
kesu assa sagāravo||
Kyassa apacitā assu||
kyāssu sādhu supūjitā ti.|| ||

13. Mātari pitari vāpi||
atho jeṭṭhamhi bhātari||
ācariye catutthamhi||
tesu na mānaɱ kayirātha.|| ||

Tesu assa sagāravo||
tyassa apacitā assu||
tyassu sādhu supūjitā.|| ||

Arahante sītibhūte||
katakicce anāsave||
nihacca mānam atthaddho||
te namassa anuttare ti.|| ||

14. Evaɱ vutte {Mānatthaddho} brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ mam bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

[page 179]

 

 

6. Paccanīka

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Paccanīkasāto nāma brāhmaṇo Sāvatthiyaɱ pativasati.|| ||

3. Atha kho Paccanīkasātassa brāhmaṇassa etad ahosi.|| ||

Yaɱ nūnāhaɱ yena samaṇo Gotamo ten-upasaŋkameyyaɱ||
yaɱ yad eva samaṇo Gotamo bhāsissati||
taɱ tad ev-assāhaɱ paccanīkassan ti.|| ||

4. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā ajjhokāse caŋkamati.|| ||

5. Atha kho Paccanīkasāto brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam caŋkamantam anucaŋkamamāno Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Bhaṇa samaṇa dhamman ti.|| ||

6. Na Paccanīkasātena||
suvijānaɱ subhāsitaɱ||
upakkiliṭṭhacittena||
sārabbhabahulena ca.|| ||

Yo ca vineyya sārabbhaɱ||
appasādañ ca cetaso||
āghātaɱ paṭinissajja||
sa ve jaññā subhāsitan ti.|| ||

7. Evaɱ vutte Paccanīkasāto brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
Upāsakam mam bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

7. Navakammika

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena navakammika-bhāradvājo brāhmaṇo tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe kammantaɱ kārāpeti.|| ||

3. Addasā kho navakammika-bhāradvājo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam aññatarasmiɱ sāla-rukkhamūle nisinnaɱ pallaŋkam ābhujitvā ujuɱ kāyaɱ paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā.|| ||

4. Disvān-assa etad ahosi|| ||

Ahaɱ kho imasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe kammantaɱ kārāpento ramāmi||
ayaɱ samaṇo Gotamo kiɱ kārāpento ramatī ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho navakammika-bhāradvājo brāhmaṇo yena

[page 180]

Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Ke nu kammantā kayiranti||
bhikkhu sālavane tava||
yad ekako araññasmiɱ||
ratiɱ vindati Gotamo ti.|| ||

6. Na me vanasmiɱ karaṇīyam atthi||
ucchinnamūlaɱ me vanaɱ visukaɱ||
so-haɱ vane nibbanatho visallo||
eko rame aratiɱ vippahāyā ti.|| ||

7. Evaɱ vutte navakammika-bhāradvājo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama||
abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

8. Kaṭṭhahāra

1. Ekam samayaɱ Bhagavā Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarasmim bhāradvājagottassa brāhmaṇassa sambahulā antevasikā kaṭṭhahārakā māṇavakā yena vaṇasaṇḍo ten-upasaŋkamiɱsu.|| ||

3. Upasaŋkamitvā addasaɱsu Bhagavantaɱ tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe nisinnaɱ pallaŋkam ābhujitvā ujuɱ kāyaɱ paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā|| ||

disvāna yena bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo ten-upasaŋkamiɱsu.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā bhāradvājagottam brāhmaṇam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Yagghe bhavaɱ jāneyya asukasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe samaṇo nisinno pallaŋkam ābhujitvā ujuɱ kāyaɱ paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā.|| ||

5. Atha kho bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo tehi māṇavakehi saddhiɱ yena so vanasaṇḍo ten-upasaŋkami||
addasā kho Bhagavantaɱ tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe nisinnaɱ pallaŋkam ābhujitvā ujuɱ kāyaɱ paṇidhāya parimukhaɱ satim upaṭṭhapetvā||
disvāna yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Gambhīrarūpe bahubherave vane||
suññam araññaɱ vijanaɱ vigāhiya||

[page 181]

aniñjamānena ṭhitena vaggunā||
sucārurupaɱ vata bhikkhu jhāyasi.|| ||

Na yattha gītaɱ na pi yattha vāditaɱ||
eko araññe vanavasito muni||
accherarūpaɱ paṭibhāti mam idaɱ||
yad ekako pītimano vane vase.|| ||

Maññe-haɱ lokādhipati-sahavyataɱ||
ākaŋkhamāno tidivam anuttaraɱ||
kasmā bhavaɱ vijanam araññam assito||
tapo idha kubbasi brahmapattiyā ti.|| ||

6. Yā kāci kaŋkhā abhinandanā vā||
anekadhātūsu puthū sadā sitā||
aññāṇamūlappabhavā pajappitā||
sabbā mayā vyantikatā samūlikā.|| ||

So ham akaŋkho apiho anupayo||
sabbesu dhammesu visuddhadassano||
pappuyya sambodhim anuttaraɱ sivaɱ||
jhāyām-ahaɱ brāhmaṇa raho visārado ti.|| ||

7. Evaɱ vutte bhāradvājagotto brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantam bho Gotama abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

9. Mātuposako

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Atha kho mātuposako brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vitisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi.|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho mātuposako brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Ahaɱ hi bho Gotama dhammena bhikkham pariyesāmi||
dhammena bhikkhaɱ pariyesitvā mātāpitaro posemi||
kaccāhaɱ bho Gotama evaɱkārī kiccakārī homī ti.|| ||

4. Taggha tvaɱ brāhmaṇa evaɱkārī kiccakārī hosi||
yo kho brāhmaṇa dhammena bhikkhaɱ pariyesati||
dhammena

[page 182]

bhikkhaɱ pariyesitvā mātāpitaro poseti||
bahu so puññam pasavatī ti.|| ||

Yo mātaraɱ pitaraɱ vā||
macco dhammena poseti||
tāya naɱ paricariyāya||
mātāpitūsu paṇḍitā||
idh-eva naɱ pasaɱsanti||
pecca sagge pamodatī ti.|| ||

5. Evaɱ vutte mātuposako brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

10. Bhikkhako

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Atha kho bhikkhako brāhmaṇo Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ sārāṇīyaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi.|| ||

3. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho bhikkhako brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Aham pi bho Gotama bhikkhako bhavam pi bhikkhako||
idha no kiɱ nānākaraṇan ti.|| ||

4. Na tena bhikkhako hoti||
yāvatā bhikkhavo pare||
visaɱ dhammam samādāya||
bhikkhu hoti na tāvatā.|| ||

Yo dha puññān ca pāpañ ca||
bāhitvā brahmacariyaɱ||
saŋkhāya loke carati||
sa ve bhikkhūti vuccatī ti.|| ||

5. Evaɱ vutte bhikkhako brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca||
Abhikkantam bho Gotama abhikkantam bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetaɱ saraṇaɱ gatan ti.|| ||

 

 

11. Saŋgārava

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Saŋgāravo nāma brāhmaṇo Sāvatthiyaɱ paṭivasati udaka-suddhiko udakena suddhim pacceti||
sāyapātam udakorohaṇānuyogam anuyutto viharati.|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthim piṇḍāya pāvisi||
Sāvatthiyaɱ piṇḍāya caritvā pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantam abhivādetvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi.|| ||

[page 183]

4. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinno kho āyasmā Ānando Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Idha bhante Saŋgāravo nāma brāhmaṇo Sāvatthiyaɱ paṭivasati udaka-suddhiko udakena suddhiɱ pacceti||
sāyapātaɱ udakorohaṇānuyogam anuyutto viharati||
sādhu bhante Bhagavā yena Saŋgāravassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaɱ ten-upasaŋkamatu anukampam upādāyā ti.|| ||

5. Adhivāsesi Bhagavā tuṇhībhāvena.|| ||

6. Atha kho Bhagavā pubbaṇha-samayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya yena Saŋgāravassa brāhmaṇassa nivesanaɱ ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā paññatte āsane nisīdi.|| ||

7. Atha kho Saŋgāravo brāhmaṇo yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavatā saddhiɱ sammodi||
sammodanīyaɱ kathaɱ vītisāretvā eka-m-antaɱ nisīdi.|| ||

8. Eka-m-antaɱ nisinnaɱ kho Saŋgāravaɱ brāhmaṇam Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

Saccaɱ kira tvaɱ brāhmaṇa udakasuddhiko udakena suddhiɱ paccesi||
sāyapātam udakorohaṇānuyogam anuyutto viharasī ti.|| ||

9. Evam bho Gotama.|| ||

10. Kam pana tvam brāhmaṇa atthavasaɱ sampassamāno udakasuddhiko udakasuddhim paccesi||
sāyapātam udakorohaṇānuyogam anuyutto viharasī ti.|| ||

11. Idha me bho Gotama ahaɱ yaɱ divā pāpakammaɱ kataɱ hoti taɱ sāyam nahānena pavāhemi||
yaɱ rattiɱ pāpakammam kataɱ hoti taɱ pātaɱ nahānena pavāhemi||
Imaɱ khvāhaɱ bho Gotama atthavasaɱ sampassamāno udakasuddhiko udakena suddhiɱ paccemi||
sāyapātam udakorohaṇānuyogam anuyutto viharāmī ti.|| ||

12. Dhammo rahado brāhmaṇa sīlatittho||
anāvilo sabbhi sataɱ pasattho||
yattha have vedaguno sinātā||
anallagattā va taranti pāran ti.|| ||

13. Evaɱ vutte Saŋgāravo brāhmaṇo Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama||
pa||
upāsakaɱ maɱ bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupetam saraṇam gatan ti.|| ||

[page 184]

 

 

12. Khomadussa

1. Evam me sutam ekam samayaɱ Bhagavā Sakkesu viharati Khomadussaɱ nāma Sakyānaɱ nigame.|| ||

2. Atha kho Bhagavā pubbaṇhasamayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Khomadussam nigamam piṇḍāya pāvisi.|| ||

3. Tena kho pana samayena Khomadussakā brāhmaṇagahapatikā sabhāyaɱ sannipatitā honti kenacid eva karaṇīyena||
devo ca ekam ekaɱ phusāyati.|| ||

4. Atha kho Bhagavā yena sā sabhā ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

5. Addasaɱsu Khomadussakā brāhmaṇa-gahapatikā Bhagavantam dūrato va āgacchantam.|| ||

6. Disvā etad avocuɱ|| ||

Ke ca muṇḍakā samaṇakā ke ca sabhādhammaɱ jānissantī ti.|| ||

7. Atha kho Bhagavā Khomadussake- brāhmaṇa-gahapatike gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

N'esā sabhā yattha na santi santo||
santo na te ye na vadanti dhammaɱ||
rāgañ ca dosañ ca pahāya mohaɱ||
dhammaɱ vadantā va bhavanti santo ti.|| ||

8. Evaɱ vutte Khomadussakā brāhmaṇa-gahapatikā Bhagavantam etad avocuɱ|| ||

Abhikkantaɱ bho Gotama abhikkantam bho Gotama||
seyyathāpi bho Gotama nikujjitaɱ vā ukujjeyya paṭicchannaɱ vā vivareyya mūḷhassa vā maggam ācikkheyya andhakāre vā telapajjotaɱ dhāreyya cakkhumanto rūpāni dakkhinti||
evam eva bhotā Gotamena anekapariyāyena dhammo pakāsito|| ||

Ete mayam Bhagavantaɱ Gotamaɱ saraṇaɱ gacchāma dhammañ ca bhikkhusaŋghañ ca||
upāsake no bhavaɱ Gotamo dhāretu ajjatagge pāṇupete saraṇaɱ gate ti.|| ||

Upāsakā-vaggo dutiyo.|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Kasi Udayo Devahito||
aññatara-Mahāsālaɱ||
Mānatthaddhaɱ Paccanīkaɱ||
Navakammi Kaṭṭhahāraɱ||
Mātuposakaɱ Bhikkhako||
Saŋgāravo Khomadussena dvādasāti.|| ||

Brāhmaṇa-saɱyuttaɱ samattaɱ.|| ||

[page 185]

 

 

Book VIII

Vaŋgīsa-Thera Saɱyuttaɱ

1. Nikkhantaɱ

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Vaŋgīso Āḷaviyaɱ viharati Aggāḷave cetiye āyasmatā NigrodhaKappena upajjhāyena saddhiɱ.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Vaŋgīso navako hoti acirapabbajito ohiyyako vihārapālo.|| ||

3. Atha kho sambahulā itthiyo samalaŋkaritvā yenārāmo ten-upasaŋkamiɱsu vihārapekkhikāyo.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa tā itthiyo disvā anabhirati upajji||
rāgo cittam anuddhaɱsesi.|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Alābhā vata me na vata me lābhā||
dulladdhaɱ vata ve na vata me suladdhaɱ||
yassa me anabhirati uppannā rāgo cittam anuddhaɱseti||
taɱ kut-ettha labbhā yam me paro anabhiratiɱ vinodetvā abhiratiɱ uppādeyya||
yaɱ nūnāham attanā va attano anabhiratiɱ vinodetvā abhiratim uppādeyyan ti.|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso attanā va attano anabhiratiɱ vinodetvā abhiratim uppādetvā tāyaɱ yelāyam imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

Nikkhantam vata maɱ santaɱ||
agārasmānagāriyaɱ||
vitakkā upadhāvanti||
pagabbhā kaṇhato ime.|| ||

Uggaputtā mahissāsā||
sikkhitā daḷhadhammino||
samantā parikireyyuɱ||
sahassam apalāyinaɱ.|| ||

Sace pi ettato bhīyo||
āgamissanti itthiyo||
n'eva maɱ vyādhayissanti||
dhamme s'amhi patiṭṭhito.|| ||

[page 186]

Sakkhī hi me sutam etaɱ||
buddhassādiccabandhuno||
nibbānagamanaɱ maggaɱ||
tattha me nirato mano.|| ||

Evañ ce maɱ viharantaɱ||
pāpima upagacchasi||
tathā maccu karissāmi||
na me maggam pi dakkasī ti.|| ||

 

 

2. Arati

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ||
la||
2. Āyasmā Vaŋgīso Āḷaviyaɱ viharati Aggāḷave cetiye āyasmatā Nigrodha-Kappena upajjhāyena saddhiɱ.|| ||

3. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Nigrodha-Kappo pacchābhattam piṇḍapātapaṭikkanto vihāram pavisati sāyaɱ vā nikkhamati aparajju vā kāle.|| ||

4. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa anabhirati uppannā hoti rāgo cittam anuddhaɱseti.|| ||

5. Atha kho Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Alābhā vata me na vata me lābhā||
dulladdhaɱ vata me na vata me suladdhaɱ||
yassa me anabhirati uppannā rāgo cittam anuddhaɱseti|| ||

Taɱ kut-ettha labbhā yaɱ me paro anabhiratiɱ vinodetvā abhiratiɱ uppādeyyan ti||
yaɱ nūnāham attanā va attano anabhiratiɱ vinodetvā abhiratim uppādeyyan ti.|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso attanā va attano anabhiratiɱ vinodetvā abhiratim uppādetvā tāyam velāyam imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

Aratiñ ca ratiñ ca pahāya||
sabbaso gehasitañ ca vitakkaɱ||
vanathaɱ na kareyya kuhiñci||
nibbanatho anato sa hi bhikkhu.|| ||

Yam idha puthaviñca vehāsaɱ||
rūpagatañ ca jagatogadhaɱ||
kiñci parijīyati sabbam aniccaɱ||
evaɱ samecca caranti mutattā.|| ||

Upadhīsu janā gadhitā||
diṭṭhasute paṭighe ca mute ca||
ettha vinodīya chandam anejo||
yo tattha na limpati tam munim āhu.|| ||

[page 187]

Atha saṭṭhitasitā vitakkā||
puthujanatāya adhammā niviṭṭhā||
na ca vaggagat-assa kuhiñci||
no pana duṭṭhullabhāṇī sa bhikkhu.|| ||

Dabbo cirarattasamāhito||
akuhako nipako apihālu||
santapadam ajjhagamā muni-paṭicca||
parinibbuto kaŋkhati kālan ti.|| ||

 

 

3. Pesalā-atimaññanā

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Vaŋgīso Āḷaviyaɱ viharati Aggāḷave cetiye āyasmatā Nigrodha-Kappena upajjhāyena saddhiɱ.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Vaŋgīso attano paṭibhānena aññe pesale bhikkhū atimaññati.|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Alābhā vata me||
na vata me lābhā||
dulladdhaɱ vata me||
na vata me suladdhaɱ||
yvāhaɱ attano paṭibhānena aññe pesale bhikkhū atimaññāmī ti.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso attanā va attano vippaṭisāram uppādetvā tāyaɱ velāyam imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

Mānaɱ pajahassu Gotama||
mānapathañ ca jahassu||
asesaɱ mānapathasmiɱ samucchito||
vippaṭisārahuvā cirarattaɱ.|| ||

Makkhena makkhitā pajā||
mānagatā nirayam papatanti||
socanti janā cirarattaɱ||
mānagatā nirayam upapannā.|| ||

Na hi socati bhikkhu kadāci||
maggajino sammāpaṭipanno.|| ||

Kittiñ ca sukhañ c' anubhoti||
dhammarato ti tam āhu tathattam.|| ||

[page 188]

Tasmā akhilo dha padhānavā||
nīvaraṇāni pahāya visuddho||
mānañ ca pahāya asesaɱ||
vijjāyantakaro samitāvī ti.|| ||

 

 

4. Ānanda

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Ānando Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando pubbaṇha-samayaɱ nivāsetvā pattacīvaram ādāya Sāvatthiɱ piṇḍāya pāvisi āyasmatā Vaŋgīsena pacchāsamaṇena.|| ||

3. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa anabhirati uppannā hoti||
rāgo cittam anuddhaɱseti.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso āyasmantam Ānandam gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Kāmarāgena ḍayhāmi||
cittam me pariḍayhati||
sādhu nibbāpanaɱ brūhi||
anukampāya Gotamā ti.|| ||

5. Saññāya vipariyesā||
cittan-te pariḍayhati||
nimittam parivajjehi||
subhaɱ rāgūpasaɱhitaɱ||
Saŋkhāre parato passa||
dukkhato mā ca attato||
nibbāpehi mahārāgaɱ||
mā ḍayhittho punappunaɱ.|| ||

Asubhāya cittaɱ bhāvehi||
ekaggaɱ susamāhitaɱ||
sati kāyagatā ty-atthu||
nibbidā-bahulo bhava.|| ||

Animittaɱ ca bhāvehi||
mānānusayam ujjaha||
tato mānābhisamayā||
upasanto carissasī ti.|| ||

 

 

5. Subhāsitā

1. Sāvatthiyaɱ Jetavane.|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Bhikkhavo ti||
3. Bhadante ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

4. Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

Catūhi bhikkhave aŋgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti na dubbhāsitā||
anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūnaɱ||
katamehi catuhi.|| ||

5. Idha bhikkhave bhikkhu subhāsitaɱ yeva bhāsati no dubbhāsitam||
dhammaɱ yeva bhāsati no adhammaɱ||

[page 189]

piyaɱ yeva bhāsati no appiyam||
saccaɱ yeva bhāsati no alikaɱ||
Imehi kho bhikkhave catūhi aŋgehi samannāgatā vācā subhāsitā hoti no dubbhāsitā anavajjā ca ananuvajjā ca viññūnan ti.|| ||

6. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
idam vatvāna Sugato athāparam etad avoca satthā.|| ||

Subhāsitam uttamam āhu santo||
dhammaɱ bhaṇe nādhammam taɱ dutiyaɱ||
piyaɱ bhaṇe nāppiyam taɱ tatiyaɱ||
saccaɱ bhaṇe nālikam tam catutthan ti.|| ||

7. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjaliɱ paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Paṭibhāti maɱ Bhagavā paṭibhāti maɱ Sugatā ti.|| ||

8. Paṭibhātu taɱ Vaŋgīsā ti Bhagavā avoca:|| ||

9. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso Bhagavantam sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Tam eva vācam bhāseyya||
yāy-attānaɱ na tāpaye||
pare ca na vihiɱseyya||
sā ve vācā subhāsitā.|| ||

Piyavācam va bhāseyya||
yā vācā paṭinanditā||
yaɱ anādāya pāpāni||
paresaɱ bhāsate piyaɱ.|| ||

Saccaɱ ve amatā vācā||
esa dhammo sanantano||
sacce atthe ca dhamme ca||
āhu santo patiṭṭhitā.|| ||

Yam buddho bhāsate vācaɱ||
khemaɱ nibbānapattiyā||
dukkhassantakiriyāya||
sā ve vācānamuttamā ti.|| ||

 

 

6. Sāriputta

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Sāriputto Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Sāriputto bhikkhū dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaɱseti||
poriyā vācāya vissaṭṭhāya anelagaḷāya atthassa viññāpaniyā||
te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhi-katvā manasi katvā sabbacetaso samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaɱ suṇanti.|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Ayam

[page 190]

āyasmā Sāriputto bhikkhū dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaɱseti||
poriyā vācāya visaṭṭhāya anelagaḷāya atthassa viññāpaniyā||
te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhikatvā manasi katvā sabba-cetaso samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaɱ suṇanti|| ||

Yaɱ nūnāham āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtaɱ sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyyan ti.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso uṭṭhayāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yenāyasmā Sāriputto tenāñjalim panāmetvā āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtam etad avoca:|| ||

Paṭibhāti mam āvuso Sāriputta paṭibhāti mam āvuso Sāriputtā ti.|| ||

5. Paṭibhātu tam āvuso Vaŋgīsā ti.|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso āyasmantaɱ Sāriputtaɱ sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Gambhīra-pañño medhāvī||
maggāmaggassa kovido.|| ||

Sāriputto mahāpañño||
dhammaɱ deseti bhikkhunaɱ.|| ||

Sakhittena pi deseti||
vitthārena pi bhāsati||
sālikāy-iva nigghoso||
paṭibhānam udīrayi.|| ||

Tassa tam desayantassa||
suṇanti madhuraɱ giraɱ||
sarena rajanīyena||
savanīyena vaggunā||
udaggacittā muditā||
sotam odhenti bhikkhavo ti.|| ||

 

 

7. Pavāraṇā

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Pubbārāme Migara-mātu-pāsāde mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeh-eva arahantehi.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā tad-ahuposathe pannarase pavāraṇāya bhikkhusaŋghaparivuto ajjhokāse nisinno hoti.|| ||

3. Atha kho Bhagavā tunhībhūtaɱ bhikkhusaŋgham anuviloketvā bhikkhū āmantesi.|| ||

4. Handa dāni bhikkhave pavārayāmi vo na ca me kiñci garahatha kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā.|| ||

5. Evaɱ vutte āyasmā Sāriputto uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgam karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjaliɱ paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Na kho mayaɱ bhante Bhagavato kiñci garahāma kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā||
Bhagavā

[page 191]

hi bhante anuppannassa maggassa uppādetā asañjātassa maggassa sañjanetā anakkhātassa maggassa akkhātā maggaññū maggavidū maggakovido maggānugā ca bhante etarahi sāvakā viharanti pacchā samannāgatā||
ahaɱ ca kho bhante Bhagavantaɱ pavāremi||
na ca me Bhagavā kiñci garahati kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā ti.|| ||

6. Na khvāhaɱ te Sāriputta kiñci garahāmi kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā||
Paṇḍito tvam Sāriputta mahāpañño tvaɱ Sāriputta puthupañño tvam Sāriputta hāsapañño tvaɱ Sāriputta javanapañño tvaɱ Sāriputta tikkhapañño tvaɱ Sāriputta nibbedhikapañño tvaɱ Sāriputta||
seyyathāpi Sāriputta rañño cakkavattissa jeṭṭhaputto pitarā pavattitaɱ cakkaɱ sammadeva anupavatteti||
evam eva kho tvaɱ Sāriputta mayā anuttaraɱ dhammacakkaɱ pavattitaɱ sammadeva anupavattesī ti.|| ||

7. No ce kira me bhante Bhagavā kiñci garahati kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā||
imesam pana bhante Bhagavā pañcannaɱ bhikkhusatānaɱ na kiñci garahati kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā ti.|| ||

8. Imesam pi khvāhaɱ Sāriputta pañcannaɱ bhikkhusatānaɱ na kiñci garahāmi kāyikaɱ vā vācasikaɱ vā||
imesam pi Sāriputta pañcannaɱ bhikkhusatānaɱ saṭṭhi bhikkhū tevijjā saṭṭhi bhikkhū chaḷabhiññā saṭṭhi bhikkhū ubhato bhāgavimuttā athā itare paññāvimuttā ti.|| ||

9. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjaliɱ paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

10. Paṭibhāti maɱ Bhagavā paṭibhāti maɱ Sugatā ti.|| ||

11. Patibhātu taɱ Vaŋgīsā ti Bhagavā avoca:|| ||

12. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso Bhagavantaɱ sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Ajja pannarase visuddhiya||
bhikkhu-pañcasatā samāgatā||
saŋyojanabandhanacchidā||
anīghā khīṇa-punabbhavā isī.|| ||

[page 192]

Cakkavatti yathā rājā||
amacca-parivārito||
samantā anupariyeti||
sāgarantaɱ mahiɱ imaɱ.|| ||

Evam vijitasaŋgāmaɱ||
satthavāham anuttaraɱ||
sāvakā payirūpāsanti||
tevijjā maccuhāyino.|| ||

Sabbe Bhagavato puttā||
palāp-ettha na vijjati||
taṇhāsallassa hantāraɱ||
vande ādiccabandhunan ti.|| ||

 

 

8. Parosahassaɱ

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme mahatā bhikkhusaŋghena saddhiɱ aḍḍhatelasehi bhikkhusatehi.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā bhikkhū nibbānapaṭisaɱyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaɱseti||
te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhi-katvā manasi katvā sabba-cetaso samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammam suṇanti.|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Ayaɱ kho Bhagavā bhikkhū nibbāna-paṭisaɱyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaɱseti||
te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhi-katvā manasi katvā sabba-cetaso samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaɱ suṇanti|| ||

Yaɱ nūnāhaɱ Bhagavantam sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyyanti.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarā saŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjaliɱ paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Paṭibhāti maɱ Bhagavā paṭibhāti mam Sugatā ti.|| ||

5. Paṭibhātu taɱ Vaŋgīsā ti Bhagavā avoca:|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso Bhagavantaɱ sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Parosahassaɱ bhikkhūnaɱ||
Sugataɱ payirūpāsati||
desentaɱ virajaɱ dhammaɱ||
nibbānam akutobhayam.|| ||

Suṇanti dhammaɱ vimalaɱ||
sammāsambuddha-desitaɱ||
sobhati vata sambuddho||
bhikkhusaŋgha-purakkhato.|| ||

Nāganāmo si Bhagavā||
isīnam isisattamo||
mahāmegho va hutvāna||
sāvake abhivassati.|| ||

[page 193]

Divāvihārā nikkhamma||
satthudassanakamyatā||
sāvako te mahāvīra||
pāde vandati Vaŋgīso ti.|| ||

7. Kin nu te Vaŋgīsa imā gāthāyo pubbe parivitakkitā udāhu ṭhānaso va taɱ paṭibhantī ti.|| ||

8. Na kho me bhante imā gāthāyo pubbe parivitakkitā atha kho ṭhānaso va maɱ paṭibhantī ti.|| ||

9. Tena hi taɱ Vaŋgīsa bhiyyosomattāya pubbe aparivitakkitā gāthāyo patibhantū ti.|| ||

10. Evam bhante ti kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso Bhagavato paṭissutvā bhiyyosomattāya Bhagavantam pubbe aparivitakkitāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Ummaggapatham Mārassa abhibhuyya||
carasi pabhijja khilāni||
tam passatha bandhapamuñcakaraɱ||
asitaɱ bhāgaso pavibhajjaɱ.|| ||

Oghassa hi nittharaṇatthaɱ||
anekavihitaɱ maggam akkhāsi||
tasmiɱ te amate akkhāte||
dhammaddasā ṭhitā asaɱhīrā.|| ||

Pajjotakaro ativijjha||
sabbaṭṭhitīnam atikkamam addasa||
ñatvā ca sacchikatvā ca||
aggaɱ so desayi dasaṭṭhānaɱ.|| ||

Evaɱ sudesite dhamme||
ko pamādo vijānataɱ dhammaɱ||
tasmā hi tassa Bhagavato sāsane||
appamatto sadā namassam anusikkhe ti.|| ||

 

 

9. Koṇḍañño

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharat: Veḷuvane kalaṇḍakanivāpe.|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmā Aññāsi-Koṇḍañño sucirasseva yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipativā Bhagavato pādāni mukhena ca paricumbati

[page 194]

pāṇīhi ca parisambāhati||
nāmañ ca sāveti Koṇḍañño-haɱ Bhagavā Koṇḍañño-ham Sugatā ti.|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Ayaɱ kho āyasmā Aññāsi-Koṇḍañño sucirasseva yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā Bhagavato pādāni mukhena ca paricumbati pāṇīhi ca parisambāhati||
nāmañ ca sāveti Koṇḍañño haɱ Bhagavā Koṇḍañño haɱ Sugatā ti|| ||

Yaɱ nūnāham āyasmatam Aññāsi-Kondaññaɱ Bhagavato sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyyan ti.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso utthāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjalim paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Paṭibhāti maɱ Bhagavā paṭibhāti maɱ Sugatā ti.|| ||

5. Paṭibhātu taɱ Vaŋgīsā ti Bhagavā avoca:|| ||

6. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso āyasmantam Aññāsi-Koṇḍaññaɱ Bhagavato sammukhā sārūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Buddhānubuddho so thero||
Koṇḍañño tibbanikkamo||
lābhī sukhavihārānaɱ||
vivekānam abhiṇhaso.|| ||

Yaɱ sāvakena pattabbam||
satthusāsana-kārinā||
sabb-assa tam anuppattaɱ||
appamattassa sikkhato.|| ||

Mahānubhāvo tevijjo||
cetopariyāya-kovido||
Koṇḍañño buddha-sāvako||
pāde vandati satthuno ti.|| ||

 

 

10. Moggallāna

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Isigilipasse Kāḷasilāyaɱ mahatā bhikkhusaŋghena saddhim pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeh-eva arahantehi||
tesaɱ sudam āyasmā Mahā-Moggallāno cetasā cittaɱ samannesati vippamuttaɱ nirupadhiɱ.|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Ayaɱ kho Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Isigili-passe Kāḷasilāyaɱ mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sabbeh-eva arahantehi||
tesaɱ sudaɱ āyasmā MahāMoggallāno cetasā cittaɱ samannesati vippamuttaɱ nirupadhiɱ|| ||

Yaɱ nūnāham āyasmantam Mahā-Moggallānaɱ Bhagavato sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthaveyyan ti.|| ||

[page 195]

3. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjaliɱ paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Paṭibhāti maɱ Bhagavā paṭibhati maɱ Sugatā ti.|| ||

4. Paṭibhātu taɱ Vaŋgīsā ti Bhagavā avoca:|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgīso āyasmantam Mahā-Moggallānam Bhagavato sammukhā sarūpāhi gāthāhi abhitthavi.|| ||

Nagassa passe āsīnaɱ||
muniɱ dukkhassa pāraguɱ||
sāvakā payirūpāsanti||
tevijjā maccuhāyino.|| ||

Te cetasā anupariyeti||
Moggalāno mahiddhiko||
cittan-nesaɱ samannesaɱ||
vippamuttam nirupadhiɱ.|| ||

Evaɱ sabbaŋgasampannaɱ||
muniɱ dukkhassa pāraguɱ||
anekākārasampannaɱ||
payirūpāsanti Gotaman ti.|| ||

 

 

11. Gaggarā

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Campāyaɱ viharati Gaggarāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ pañcamattehi bhikkhu-satehi sattahi ca upāsaka-satehi sattahi ca upāsika-satehi anekehi ca devatā-sahassehi||
tyāssudaɱ Bhagavā atirocati vaṇṇena c-eva yasasā ca.|| ||

2. Atha kho āyasmato Vaŋgīsassa etad ahosi|| ||

Ayaɱ kho Bhagavā Campāyaɱ viharati Gaggarāya pokkharaṇiyā tīre mahatā bhikkhu-saŋghena saddhiɱ pañcamattehi bhikkhusatehi sattahi ca upāsakasatehi sattahi ca upāsikasattehi anekehi ca devatā-sahassehi||
tyāssudaɱ Bhagavā atirocati vaṇṇena c-eva yasasā ca|| ||

Yaɱ nūnāhaɱ Bhagavantaɱ sammukkā sarūpāya gāthāya abhitthaveyyanti.|| ||

3. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgiso uṭṭhāyāsanā ekaɱsam uttarāsaŋgaɱ karitvā yena Bhagavā ten-añjalim paṇāmetvā Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Paṭibhāti maɱ Bhagavā paṭibhāti maɱ Sugatā ti.|| ||

4. Paṭibhātu taɱ Vaŋgisā ti Bhagavā avoca:|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Vaŋgiso Bhagavato sammukhā sarūpāya gāthāya abhitthavi.|| ||

[page 196]

Cando yathā vigatavalāhake nabhe||
virocati vītamalo va bhāṇumā||
evam pi Aŋgīrassa tvaɱ mahāmuni||
atirocasi yasasā sabbalokan ti.|| ||

 

 

12. Vaŋgīsa

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Vaŋgīso aciraarahattappatto hutvā vimutti-sukha-{paṭisaɱvedī} tāyaɱ velāyaɱ imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

Kāveyyamattā vicarimha pubbe||
gāmāgamam purāpuraɱ||
ath'addasāma sambuddhaɱ||
saddhā no udapajjatha.|| ||

So me dhammam adesesi||
khandhe āyatānāni||
dhātuyo ca||
tassāhaɱ dhammaɱ sutvāna||
pabbajiɱ anagāriyaɱ.|| ||

Bahunnam vata atthāya||
bodhim ajjhagamā muni||
bhikkhūnaɱ bhikkhunīnañ ca||
ye niyāmagataddasā.|| ||

Svāgataɱ vata me asi||
mama buddhassa santike||
tisso vijjā anuppattā||
kataɱ buddhassa sāsanan ti.|| ||

Pubbe-nivāsaɱ jānāmi||
dibbacakkhuɱ visodhitaɱ||
tevijjo iddhippattomhi||
cetopariyāya-kovido ti.|| ||

Vaŋgīsa-thera-saɱyuttaɱ.|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Nikkhantam Arati c-eva||
Pesalā-atimaññanā||
Ānandena Subhāsitā||
Sāriputta Pavāraṇā||
Parosahassaɱ Kondañño||
Moggalānena Gaggarā||
Vaŋgīsena dvādasāti.|| ||

[page 197]

 

 

Book IX

Vana Saɱyutta

1. Viveka

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena- so bhikkhu divāvihāragato pāpake akusale vitakke vitakketi gehanissite
3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taɱ bhikkhuɱ saɱvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā taɱ bhikkhuɱ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Vivekakāmo si vanaɱ paviṭṭho||
atha te mano niccharati bhahiddhā||
jano janasmiɱ vinayassu chandaɱ||
tato sukhī bohisi vītarāgo.|| ||

Aratim pajahāsi so sato||
bhavāsi sataɱ taɱ sārayāmase||
pātālarajo hi duruttamo||
mā tam kāmarajo avāhari.|| ||

Sakuṇo yathā paɱsukuṇḍito||
vidhūnaɱ pātayati sitaɱ rajaɱ||
evam bhikkhu padhānavā satimā||
vidhūnaɱ pātayati sitam rajan ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saɱvejito saɱvegam āpādī ti.|| ||

 

 

2. Upaṭṭhāna

1. Ekaɱ samayam aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

[page 198]

2. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu divāvihāragato supati.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taɱ bhikkhuɱ saɱvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā taɱ bhikkhuɱ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Uṭṭhehi bhikkhu kiɱ sesi||
ko attho supitena te||
āturassa hi kā niddā||
sallaviddhassa ruppato||
yāya saddhāya pabbajito||
agārasmānagāriyaɱ||
tam eva saddhaɱ brūhehi||
mā niddāya vasaɱ gamī ti.|| ||

5. Aniccā addhuvā kāmā||
yesu mando samucchito||
bandhesu muttam asitaɱ||
kasmā pabbajitaɱ tape.|| ||

Chandarāgassa vinayā||
avijjāsamatikkamā||
taɱ ñāṇam pariyodātaɱ||
kasmā pabbajitaɱ tape.|| ||

Bhetvā avijjaɱ vijjāya||
āsavānaɱ parikkhayā||
asokam anupāyāsaɱ||
kasmā pabbajitaɱ tape.|| ||

Āraddhaviriyam pahitattaɱ||
niccaɱ daḷhaparakkamaɱ||
nibbānaɱ abhikaŋkhantaɱ||
kasmā pabbajitaɱ tapeti.|| ||

 

 

3. Kassapagotta (or Cheta)

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Kassapagotto Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Kassapagotto divāvihāragato aññataraɱ chetaɱ ovadati.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā āyasmato Kassapagottassa anukampikā atthakāmā āyasmantaɱ Kassapagottaɱ {saɱvejetukāmā} yenāyasmā Kassapagotto tenupasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Kassapagottaɱ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Giriduggacaraɱ chetaɱ||
appapaññam acetasaɱ||
akāle ovādaɱ bhikkhu||
mando va paṭibhāti maɱ.|| ||

Suṇoti na vijānāti||
āloketi na passati||
dhammasmiɱ bhaññamānasmiɱ||
atthaɱ bālo na bujjhati.|| ||

[page 199]

sace pi dasa pajjote||
dhārayissasi Kassapa||
n'eva dakkhiti rūpāni||
cakkhu hi-ssa na vijjatī ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Kassapagotto tāya devatāya saɱvejito saɱvegam āpādī ti.|| ||

 

 

4. Sambahulā (or Cārika)

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ sambahulā bhikkhū Kosalesu viharanti aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Atha kho te bhikkhū vassaɱ vutthā temāsaccayena cārikaɱ pakkamiɱsu.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā te bhikkhū apassantī paridevamānā tāyaɱ velāyaɱ imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Arati viya me-jja khāyati||
bahuke disvāna vivitte āsane||
te cittakathā bahussutā||
ko-me Gotama-savakā gatā ti.|| ||

4. Evaɱ vutte aññatarā devatā taɱ devataɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Magadhaɱ gatā Kosalaɱ gatā||
ekacciyā pana Vajja-bhūmiyā||
magā viya asaŋgacārino||
aniketā viharanti bhikkhavo ti.|| ||

 

 

5. Ānando

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Ānando Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Ānando ativelaɱ gihisaññattibahulo viharati.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā āyasmato Ānandassa anukampikā atthakāmā āyasmantam Ānandam saɱvejetukāmā yenāyasmā Ānando ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantam Ānandaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Rukkhamūlagahanaɱ pasakkiya||
nibbānaɱ hadayasmiɱ opiya||

[page 200]

jhāya Gotama mā ca pamādo||
kiɱ te biḷibiḷikā karissatī ti.|| ||

4. Atha kho āyasmā Ānando tāya devatāya saɱvejito saɱvegam āpādī ti.|| ||

 

 

6. Anuruddho

1. Ekaɱ samayam āyasmā Anuruddho Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Atha kho aññatarā Tāvatiɱsa-kāyikā devatā Jālinī nāma āyasmato Anuruddhassa purāṇa-dutiyikā yenāyasmā Anuruddho ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

3. Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantam Anuruddhaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Tattha cittam paṇidhehi||
yattha te vusitaɱ pure||
Tāvatiɱsesu devesu||
sabbakāmasamiddhisu||
purakkhato parivuto||
devakaññāhi sobhasi.|| ||

4. Duggatā devakaññāyo||
sakkāyasmiɱ patiṭṭhitā||
te cāpi duggatā sattā||
devakaññābhipattikā.|| ||

5. Na te sukham pajānanti||
ye na passanti Nandanaɱ||
āvāsaɱ naradevānaɱ||
tidasānam yasassinan ti.|| ||

6. Na tvam bāle vijānāsi||
yathā arahataɱ vaco||
aniccā sabbe saŋkhārā||
uppadavayadhammino||
uppajjitvā nirujjhanti||
tesaɱ vūpasamo sukho.|| ||

Natthidāni punāvāso||
devakāyasmiɱ Jālinī||
vikkhīṇo jātisaɱsāro||
natthi dāni punabbhavo ti.|| ||

 

 

7. Nāgadatta

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ āyasmā Nāgadatto Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Nāgadatto atikālena gāmaɱ pavisati atidivā paṭikkamati.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā āyasmato Nāgadattassa anukampikā atthakāmā āyasmantaɱ Nāgadattam saɱvejetu-kāmā yenāyasmā Nāgadatto ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

[page 201]

4. Upasaŋkamitvā āyasmantaɱ Nāgadattaɱ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Kāle pavissa Nāgadatta
divā ca āgantvā ativela-||
cārī saɱsaṭṭho gahaṭṭhehi||
samānasukhadukkho.|| ||

Bhāyāmi Nāgadattaɱ suppagabbhaɱ||
kulesu vinibandhaɱ||
mā heva maccurañño balavato||
antakassa vasam eyyā ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho āyasmā Nāgadatto tāya devatāya saɱvejito {saɱvegam} āpādī ti.|| ||

 

 

8. Kulagharaṇī (or Ogāḷho)

1. Ekaɱ samayam aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu aññatarasmiɱ kule ativelam ajjhogāḷhappatto viharati.|| ||

3. Atha kho tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā tam bhikkhuɱ saɱvejetu-kāmā yā tasmiɱ kule kulagharaṇī tassā vaṇṇam abhinimminitvā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā taɱ bhikkhuɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Nadītīresu saṇṭhāne sabhāsu rathiyāsu ca||
janā saŋgamma mantenti||
mañ ca tañ ca kim antaran-
ti.|| ||

5. Bahū hi saddā paccūhā||
khamitabbā tapassinā||
na tena maŋkuhotabbo||
na hi tena kilissati.|| ||

Yo ca saddaparittāsī||
vane vātamigo yathā||
lahucitto ti tam āhu||
nāssa sampajjate vatan ti.|| ||

 

 

9. Vajjiputto (or Vesālī)

1. Ekaɱ samayam aññataro Vajjiputtako bhikkhu Vesaliyaɱ viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Vesāliyaɱ sabbaratti-cāro hoti.|| ||

[page 202]

3. Atha kho so bhikkhu Vesāliyaɱ turiya-tāḷita-vāditanighosa-saddaɱ sutvā paridevamāno tāyaɱ velāyaɱ imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Ekakā mayam araññe viharāma||
apaviddhaɱ va vanasmiɱ dārukaɱ||
etadisikāya rattiyā||
ko sunāma amhehi pāpiyo ti.|| ||

4. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taɱ bhikkhuɱ saɱvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

5. Upasaŋkamitvā tam bhikkhuɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Ekako tvaɱ araññe viharasi||
apaviddhaɱ va vanasmiɱ dārukaɱ||
tassa te bahukā pihayanti||
nerayikā viya saggagaminan ti.|| ||

6. Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saɱvejito {saɱvegam} apādī ti.|| ||

 

 

10. Sajjhāya (or Dhamma)

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu yaɱ sudaɱ pubbe ativelaɱ sajjhāya bahulo viharati||
so aparena samayena appossukko tuṇhībhūto saŋkasāyati.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno dhammam asuṇantī yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā taɱ bhikkhuɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Kasmā tuvaɱ dhammapadāni bhikkhu||
nādhīyasi bhikkhūhi saɱvasanto||
sutvāna dhammaɱ labhati-ppasādaɱ||
diṭṭheva dhamme labhati-ppasaɱsan ti.|| ||

5. Ahu pure dhammapadesu chando||
yāva virāgena samāgamimha||

[page 203]

yato virāgena samāgamimha||
yaɱ kiñci diṭṭhaɱ va sutaɱ va mutaɱ||
aññāya nikkhepanam āhu santo ti.|| ||

 

 

11. Ayoniso (or Vitakkita)

1. Ekaɱ samayam aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu divāvihāragato pāpake akusale vitakke vitakketi||
seyyathīdaɱ kāmavitakkaɱ vyāpāda-vitakkaɱ vihiɱsa-vitakkaɱ.|| ||

3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā tam bhikkhuɱ saɱvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā tam bhikkhuɱ gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Ayoniso manasikārā||
bho vitakkehi majjasi||
ayoniɱ paṭinissajja||
yoniso anuvicintaya.|| ||

Satthāraɱ dhammam ārabbha||
saŋgham sīlānivattano||
adhigacchasi pāmojjaɱ||
pītisukham asaɱsayaɱ||
tato pāmojjabahulo||
dukkhass-antaɱ karissasī ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya saɱvejito saɱvegam āpādī ti.|| ||

 

 

12. Majjhantiko (or Saṇika)

1. Ekaɱ samayam aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

3. Upasaŋkamitvā tassa bhikkhuno santike imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Ṭhite majjhantike kāle||
sannisinnesu pakkhisu||
saṇateva mahāraññaɱ||
taɱ bhayaɱ paṭibhāti maɱ.|| ||

4. Ṭhite majjhantike kāle||
sannisinnesu pakkhisu||
saṇateva mahāraññaɱ||
sā rati patibhāti man ti.|| ||

 

 

13. Pākatindriya (or Sambahulā bhikkhū)

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ sambahulā bhikkhū Kosalesu viharanti aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe uddhatā uṇṇaḷā capalā mukharā

[page 204]

vikiṇṇavācā muṭṭhassatino asampajānā asamāhitā vibbhantacittā pākatindriyā.|| ||

2. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tesam bhikkhūnaɱ anukampikā atthakāmā te bhikkhū saɱvejetukāmā yena te bhikkhū ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

3. Upasaŋkamitvā te bhikkhū gāthāhi ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Sukhajīvino pure āsuɱ||
bhikkhū Gotama-sāvakā||
anicchā piṇḍam esanā||
anicchā sayanāsanaɱ||
loke aniccataɱ ñatvā||
dukkhass-antam akaɱsu te.|| ||

Dupposaɱ katvā attānam||
gāme gāmaṇikā viya||
bhutvā bhutvā nipajjanti||
parāgāresu mucchitā||
saŋghassa añjaliɱ katvā||
idh-ekacce vadām-ahaɱ.|| ||

Appaviddhā anāthā te||
yathā petā tath-eva te||
ye kho pamattā viharanti||
te me sandhāya bhāsitaɱ||
ye appamattā viharanti||
namo tesaɱ karom-ahanti.|| ||

4. Atha kho te bhikkhū tāya devatāya saɱvejitā saɱvegam āpādun ti.|| ||

 

 

14. Paduma-puppha (or Puṇḍarīka)

1. Ekaɱ samayam aññataro bhikkhu Kosalesu viharati aññatarasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena so bhikkhu pacchābhattaɱ piṇḍapātapatikkanto pokkharaṇim ogahetvā padumam upasiŋghati||
3. Atha kho yā tasmiɱ vanasaṇḍe adhivatthā devatā tassa bhikkhuno anukampikā atthakāmā taɱ bhikkhuɱ saɱvejetukāmā yena so bhikkhu ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

4. Upasaŋkamitvā taɱ bhikkhuɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Yam etaɱ vārijaɱ pupphaɱ||
adinnam upasiŋghasi||
ekaŋgam etaɱ theyyānaɱ||
gandhattheno si mārisā ti.|| ||

5. Na harāmi na bhañjāmi||
ārā siŋghāmi vārijaɱ||
atha kena nu vaṇṇena||
gandhattheno ti vuccati.|| ||

Yvāyaɱ bhisāni khaṇati||
puṇḍarīkāni bhuñjati||
evam ākiṇṇakammanto||
kasmā eso na vuccati.|| ||

[page 205]

6. ākiṇṇaluddo puriso||
dhāti celaɱ va makkhito||
tasmiɱ me vacanaɱ natthi||
tañ cārahāmi vattave.|| ||

Anaŋgaṇassa posassa||
niccaɱ sucigavesino||
vāḷaggamattam pāpassa||
abbhāmattaɱ va khāyati.|| ||

7. addhā maɱ yakkha jānāsi||
atho mam anukampasi||
puna pi yakkha vajjesi||
yadā passasi edisaɱ.|| ||

8. neva taɱ upājīvāmi||
na pi te katakammase||
tvam eva bhikkhu jāneyya||
yena gaccheyya suggatin ti.|| ||

9. Atha kho so bhikkhu tāya devatāya {saɱvejito} {saɱvegam} āpādī ti.|| ||

Vana-saɱyuttaɱ samattaɱ.|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Viveka Uppaṭṭhānañ ca||
Kassapagottena ca||
Sambahulā Ānando||
Anuruddho Nāgadattañ ca||
Kulagharanī Vajjīputto||
Vesalī Sajjhāyena ca||
Ayoniso Majjhantikālamhi ca||
Pākatindriya-padumapupphena cuddasa bhaveti.|| ||

[page 206]

 

 

Book X

Yakkha Saɱyuttaɱ

1. Indako

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Indakūṭe pabbate Indakassa yakkhassa bhavane.|| ||

2. Atha kho Indako yakkho yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Rūpaɱ na jīvan ti vadanti buddhā||
kathaɱ nvayaɱ vindat-imaɱ sarīraɱ||
kut-assa aṭṭhīyakapiṇḍam eti||
kathaɱ nvayaɱ sajjati gabbharasmin ti.|| ||

3. Pathamaɱ kalalaɱ hoti||
kalalā hoti abbudaɱ||
abbudā jāyate pesī||
pesī nibbattati ghano||
ghanā pasākhā jāyanti||
kesā lomā nakhāni ca.|| ||

Yañ c-assa bhuñjati māta||
annam pānañ ca bhojanaɱ||
tena so tattha yāpeti||
mātukucchigato naro ti.|| ||

 

 

2. Sakka

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Gijjhakūṭe pabbate||
2. Atha kho Sakka-nāmako yakkho yena Bhagavā tenupasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavantaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Sabbaganthapahīnassa||
vippamuttassa te sato||
samaṇassa na taɱ sādhu||
yad aññam anusāsatī ti.|| ||

3. Yena kenaci vaṇṇena||
saɱvāso Sakka jāyati||
na tam arahati sappañño||
manasā anukampituɱ.|| ||

Manasā ce pasannena||
yad aññam anusāsati||
na tena hoti saɱyutto||
sānukampā anuddayā ti.|| ||

[page 207]

 

 

3. Sucilomo

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Gayāyaɱ viharati Ṭaŋkitamañce Suciloma-yakkhassa bhavane.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Kharo ca yakkho Sucilomo ca yakkho Bhagavato avidūre atikkamanti.|| ||

3. Atha kho Kharo yakkho Sucilomaɱ yakkham etad avoca:|| ||

Eso samaṇo ti.|| ||

4. N'esā samaṇo samaṇako eso||
yāva jānāmi yadi vā so samaṇo yadi vā pana so samaṇako ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho Sucilomo yakkho yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato kāyam upanāmesi.|| ||

6. Atha kho Bhagavā kāyam apanāmesi||
7. Atha kho Sucilomo yakkho Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Bhāyasi maɱ samaṇā ti.|| ||

8. Na khvāhaɱ taɱ āvuso bhāyāmi||
api ca te samphasso pāpako ti.|| ||

9. Pañhaɱ taɱ samaṇa pucchissāmi||
sace me na vyākarissasi||
cittaɱ vā te khipissāmi hadayaɱ vā te phālessāmi||
pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaŋgāya khipissāmī ti.|| ||

10. Na khvāhaɱ taɱ āvuso passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇa-brāhmaṇiyā pajāya sa devamanussāya yo me cittaɱ va khipeyya hadayaɱ vā phāleyya||
pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaŋgāya khipeyya||
api ca tvam āvuso puccha yad ākaŋkhasī ti.|| ||

11. Rāgo ca doso ca kuto nidānā||
arati rati lomahaɱso kutojā||
kuto samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā||
kumārakā dhaŋkam iv-ossajantī ti.|| ||

12. Rāgo ca doso ca ito nidānā||
arati rati lomahaɱso itojā||
ito samuṭṭhāya manovitakkā||
kumārakā dhaŋkam iv-ossajanti.|| ||

Snehajā attasambhūtā||
nigrodhasseva khandhajā||
puthū visattā kāmesu||
māluvā va vitatā vane.|| ||

[page 208]

Ye naɱ pajānanti yato nidānaɱ||
te naɱ vinodenti suṇohi yakkha||
te duttaram ogham imaɱ taranti||
atiṇṇapubbaɱ apunabbhavāyā ti.|| ||

 

 

4. Maṇibhaddo

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Magadhesu viharati Maṇimālake cetiye Maṇibhaddassa yakkhassa bhavane.|| ||

2. Atha kho Maṇibhaddo yakkho yena Bhagavā ten-upasaŋkami||
upasaŋkamitvā Bhagavato santike imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

[Satimato sadā bhaddaɱ||
satimā sukham edhati||
satimato su ve seyyo||
verā ca parimuccatī ti].|| ||

3. Satimato sadā bhaddaɱ||
satimā sukham edhati||
satimato su ve seyyo||
verā na parimuccati.|| ||

Yassa sabbam ahorattam||
ahiɱsāya rato mano||
mettaɱ so sabbabhūtesu||
veraɱ tassa na kenacī ti.|| ||

 

 

5. Sānu

1. Ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Sāvatthiyam viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena aññatarissā upāsikāya Sānu nāma putto yakkhena gahito hoti.|| ||

3. Atha kho sā upasikā paridevamānā tāyaɱ velāyam imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

[Sā hūti me arahataɱ||
iti me arahataɱ sutaɱ||
sā dāni ajja passāmi||
yakkhā kīḷanti Sānunā ti].|| ||

Cātuddasiɱ pañcaddasiɱ||
yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamī||
pāṭihāriyapakkhañca||
aṭṭhaŋga-susamāhitaɱ.|| ||

Uposatham upavasanti||
iti me arahataɱ sutaɱ||
sā dāni ajja passāmi||
yakkhā kīḷanti Sānunā ti.|| ||

Cātuddasim pañcaddasiɱ||
yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamī||
pātihāriyapakkhañca||
aṭṭhaŋga-susamāhitaɱ.|| ||

[page 209]

Uposatham upavasanti||
brahmacariyaɱ caranti ye||
na tehi yakkhā kīḷanti||
iti me arahataɱ sutaɱ.|| ||

Sāṇuɱ pabuddhaɱ vajjāsi||
yakkhānaɱ vacanam idam||
mā kāsi pāpakam kammam||
āviɱ vā yadivā raho.|| ||

Sac'eva pāpakaɱ kammaɱ||
karissasi karosi vā||
na te dukkhā pamuty-atthi||
uppaccāpi palāyato ti.|| ||

4. Mataɱ va amma rodanti||
yo vā jīvaɱ na dissati||
jīvantam amma passantī||
kasmā mam amma rodasī ti.|| ||

5. Mataɱ va puttam rodanti||
yo vā jīvam na dissati||
yo ca kāmeva jitvāna||
punar āgacchate idha||
taɱ vāpi putta rodanti||
puna jīvaɱ mato hi so.|| ||

Kukkuḷā ubbhato tāta||
kukkuḷam patitum icchasi||
narakā ubbhato tāta||
narakam patitum icchasi||
abhidhāvatha bhaddan-te||
kassa ujjhāpayāmase||
ādittā nibhataɱ bhaṇḍaɱ||
puna ḍayhitum icchasī ti.|| ||

 

 

6. Piyaŋkara

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ āyasmā Anuruddho Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme||
2. Tena kho pana samayena āyasmā Anuruddho rattiyā paccūsasamayaɱ paccuṭṭhāya dhammapadāni bhāsati.|| ||

3. Atha kho Piyaŋkara-mātā yakkhinī puttakam evaɱ tosesi.|| ||

Mā saddaɱ karī Piyaŋkara||
bhikkhu dhammapadāni bhāsati||
api ca dhammapadaɱ vijānīya||
paṭipajjema hitāya no siyā.|| ||

Pāṇesu ca saɱyamāmase||
sampajānamusā na bhaṇāmase||
sikkhema susīlyam attano||
api muccema pisāca-yoniyā ti.|| ||

 

 

7. Punabbasu

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

[page 210]

2. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā bhikkhū nibbānapaṭisaɱyuttāya dhammiyā kathāya sandasseti samādapeti samuttejeti sampahaɱseti||
te ca bhikkhū aṭṭhi-katvā manasi katvā sabbaɱ cetasā samannāharitvā ohitasotā dhammaɱ suṇanti.|| ||

3. Atha kho Punabbasu-mātā yakkhinī puttake evam toseti.|| ||

Tuṇhī Uttarike hohi||
tuṇhi hohi Punabbasu||
yāvāhaɱ buddhaseṭṭhassa||
dhammaɱ sossāmi satthuno.|| ||

Nibbānaɱ Bhagavā āhu||
sabbaganthappamocanaɱ||
ativelā ca me hoti||
asmiɱ dhamme piyāyanā.|| ||

Piyo loke sako putto||
piyo loke sako pati||
tato piyatarā mayhaɱ||
assa dhammassa magganā.|| ||

Na hi putto pati vā pi||
piyo dukkhā pamocaye||
yathā saddhammasavanaɱ||
dukkhā moceti pāṇinaɱ.|| ||

Loke dukkhapare tasmiɱ||
jarāmaraṇasaɱyutte||
jarāmaraṇamokkhāya||
yaɱ dhammam abhisambuddhaɱ||
taɱ dhammaɱ sotum icchāmi||
tuṇhī hohi Punabbasū ti.|| ||

4. Amma na vyāharissāmi||
tuṇhībhūtāyam Uttarā||
dhammam eva nisāmehi||
saddhamasavanaɱ sukhaɱ||
saddhammassa anaññāya||
amma dukkhaɱ carāmase.|| ||

Esa devamanussānaɱ||
sammūḷhānam pabhaŋkaro||
buddho antimasarīro||
dhammaɱ deseti cakkhumā.|| ||

5. Sādhu kho paṇḍito nāma||
putto jāto ure seyyo||
putto me buddhaseṭṭhassa||
dhammaɱ suddham piyāyati.|| ||

Punabbasu sukhī hohi||
ajjāhamhi samuggatā||
diṭṭhāni ariyasaccāni||
Uttarā pi suṇatu me ti.|| ||

 

 

8. Sudatto

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Sītavane.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati Rājagaham anuppatto hoti kenacid eva karaṇīyena.|| ||

3. Assosi kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati buddho kiro loke uppanno ti||
tāvad eva pana Bhagavantam dassanāya upasaŋkamitu-kāmo ahosi||

[page 211]

4. Ath-assa Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa etad ahosi.|| ||

Akālo kho ajja Bhagavantaɱ dassanāya upasaŋkamituɱ||
svedānāhaɱ kālena Bhagavantaɱ dassanāya upasaŋkamissāmīti buddhagatāya satiyā nipajji||
rattiyā sudaɱ tikkhattuɱ vuṭṭhāsi pabhātan ti maññamāno.|| ||

5. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati yena Sīvathikadvāraɱ ten-upasaŋkami||
amanussā dvāraɱ vivariɱsu.|| ||

6. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa nagaramhā nikkhamantassa āloko antaradhāyi andhakāro pātur ahosi||
bhayaɱ chambhitattaɱ lomahaɱso udapādi||
tato ca puna nivattitu-kāmo ahosi.|| ||

7. Atha kho Sīvako yakkho antarahito saddam anussāvesi.|| ||

Sataɱ hatthī satam assā||
satam assasarī rathā||
sataɱ kaññā-sahassāni||
āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā||
ekassa padavītihārassa||
kalam nāgghanti solasiɱ.|| ||

Abhikkama gahapati||
abhikkama gahapati||
abhikkamanan-te seyyo||
na paṭikkamanan ti.|| ||

8. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa andhakāro antaradhāyi āloko pātur ahosi||
Yam ahosi bhayaɱ chambhitattam lomahaɱso so paṭipassambhi.|| ||

9. Dutiyam pi kho||
pe|||| ||

10. Tatiyam pi Anāthapiṇḍikassa āloko antaradhāyi andhakāre pātur ahosi||
bhayaɱ chambhitattam lomahaɱso udapādi||
tato ca puna nivattitukāmo ahosi.|| ||

Tatiyam pi kho Sīvako yakkho antarahito saddam anussāvesi.|| ||

Satam hatthī satam assā||
satam assasarī rathā||
sataɱ kaññāsahassāni||
āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā||
ekassa padavītihārassa||
kalaɱ nāgghanti soḷasiɱ.|| ||

Abhikkama gahapati||
abhikkama gahapati||
abhikkamanan-te seyyo||
no patikkamanan ti.|| ||

11. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍikassa gahapatissa andhakāro

[page 212]

antaradhāyi āloko pātur ahosi||
yaɱ ahosi bhayaɱ chambhitattaɱ lomahaɱso so paṭippassambhi.|| ||

12. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati yena Sītavanaɱ [yena Bhagavā] ten-upasaŋkami.|| ||

13. Tena kho pana samayena Bhagavā rattiyā paccūsasamayaɱ paccuṭṭhāya ajjhokāse caŋkamati.|| ||

14. Addasā kho Bhagavā Anāthapiṇḍikaɱ gahapatiɱ dūrato va āgacchantaɱ||
disvāna caŋkamā orohitvā paññatte āsane nisidi||
nisajja kho Bhagavā Anāthapiṇḍikam gahapatim etad avoca:|| ||

Ehi Sudattā ti.|| ||

15. Atha kho Anāthapiṇḍiko gahapati nāmena maɱ Bhagavā ālapatīti tatth-eva Bhagavato pādesu sirasā nipatitvā bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Kacci bhante Bhagavā sukham asayitthā ti.|| ||

Sabbadā ve sukhaɱ seti||
brāhmaṇo parinibbuto||
yo na limpati kāmesu||
sītibhūto nirupadhi.|| ||

Sabbā āsattiyo chetvā||
vineyya hadaye daraɱ||
upasanto sukhaɱ seti||
santim pappuyya cetasā ti.|| ||

 

 

9. Sukkā (1)

1. Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane kalandaka-nivāpe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena Sukkā bhikkhunī mahatiyā parisāya parivutā dhammam deseti.|| ||

3. Atha kho Sukkāya bhikkhuniyā abhippasanno yakkho Rājagahe rathikāya rathikam siŋghāṭakena siŋghāṭakam upasaŋkamitvā tāyaɱ velāyam imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

Kim me katā Rājagahe manussā||
madhupītā va acchare ye||
Sukkam na payirūpāsanti||
desentim amataɱ padaɱ.|| ||

Tañ ca pana appaṭivānīyaɱ||
asecanakam ojavaɱ||
pivanti maññe sappaññā||
valāhakam iva panthagūti.|| ||

 

 

10. Sukkā (2)

1. Ekam samayaɱ Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane kalandakanivāpe||

[page 213]

2. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro upāsako Sukkāya bhikkhuniyā bhojanam adāsi.|| ||

3. Atha kho Sukkāya bhikkhuniyā abhippasanno yakkho Rājagahe rathikāya rathikaɱ siŋghāṭakena siŋghāṭakaɱ upasaŋkamitvā tāyaɱ velāyam imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Puññaɱ vata pasavi bahuɱ||
sapañño vatāyam upāsako||
yo Sukkāya adāsi bhojanaɱ||
sabbaganthehi vippamuttiyā ti.|| ||

 

 

11. Cīrā (or Vīrā)

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Rājagahe viharati Veḷuvane kalandaka-nivāpe.|| ||

2. Tena kho pana samayena aññataro upāsako Cīrāya bhikkhuniyā cīvaram adāsi.|| ||

3. Atha kho Cīrāya bhikkhuniyā abhippasanno yakkho Rājagahe rathikāya rathikaɱ siŋghāṭakena siŋghāṭakaɱ upasaŋkamitvā tayam velāyam imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Puññam vata pasavi bahuɱ||
sapañño vatāyam upāsako||
yo Cīrāya adāsi cīvaraɱ||
sabbayogehi vippamuttiyā ti.|| ||

 

 

12. Āḷavam

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayam Bhagavā Āḷaviyam viharati Āḷavakassa yakkhassa bhavane.|| ||

2. Atha kho Āḷavako yakkho Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Nikkhama samaṇā ti.|| ||

Sādh'āvuso ti Bhagavā nikkhami.|| ||

Pavisa samaṇā ti||
Sādh'āvuso ti Bhagavā pāvisi.|| ||

3. Dutiyam pi kho Āḷavako yakkho Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Nikkhama samaṇā ti|| ||

Sādh'āvuso ti Bhagavā nikkhami|| ||

Pavisa samaṇā ti|| ||

Sādh'āvuso ti Bhagavā pāvisi.|| ||

[page 214]

4. Tatiyam pi kho Āḷavako yakkho Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Nikkhama samaṇā ti|| ||

Sādh'āvuso ti Bhagavā nikkhami|| ||

Pavisa samaṇāti|| ||

Sādh'āvuso ti Bhagavā pāvisi.|| ||

5. Catuttham pi kho Āḷavako yakkho Bhagavantam etad avoca:|| ||

Nikkhama samaṇā ti.|| ||

6. Na kho panāham āvuso nikkhamissāmi||
yan-te karaṇīyaɱ taɱ karohī ti.|| ||

7. Pañhaɱ taɱ samaṇa pucchissāmi||
sace me na karissasi cittam vā te khipissāmi hadayaɱ vā te phālessāmi pādesu vā gahetvā pāraganāya khipissāmī ti.|| ||

8. Na khvāhan-tam āvuso passāmi sadevake loke samārake sabrahmake sassamaṇa-brāhmaṇiyā pajāya sadevamanussāya yo me cittam vā khipeyya hadayaɱ vā phāleyya pādesu vā gahetvā pāragaŋgāya khippeya||
api ca tvam āvuso puccha yad ākaŋkhasī ti.|| ||

9. Kiɱ sūdha vittam purisassa seṭṭhaɱ||
kiɱ su suciṇṇam sukham āvahāti||
kiɱ su have sādutaraɱ rasānam||
kathaɱ jīviɱ jīvitam āhu seṭṭhan ti.|| ||

10. Saddhidha vittam purisassa seṭṭhaɱ||
dhammo suciṇṇo sukham āvahāti||
saccam have sādutaraɱ rasānaɱ||
paññājīviɱ jīvitam āhu seṭṭhanti.|| ||

11. Kathaɱ su tarati oghaɱ||
kathaɱ su tarati aṇṇavaɱ||
kathaɱ su dukkham acceti||
kathaɱ su parisujjhatī ti.|| ||

12. Saddhāya tarati oghaɱ||
appamādena aṇṇavaɱ||
viriyena dukkham acceti||
paññāya parisujjhati.|| ||

13. Kathaɱ su labhate paññaɱ||
kathaɱ su vindate dhanaɱ.|| ||

Kathaɱ su kittim pappoti||
katham mittāni ganthati||
asmā lokā paraɱ lokaɱ||
katham pecca na socatī ti.|| ||

14. Saddahāno arahataɱ||
dhammaɱ nibbānapattiyā||
sussūsā labhate paññaɱ||
appamatto vicakkhaṇo.|| ||

Paṭirūpakārī dhuravā||
uṭṭhātā vindate dhanaɱ||

[page 215]

saccena kittim pappoti||
dadaɱ mittāni ganthati.|| ||

Asmā lokā paraɱ lokaɱ||
evam pecca na socati.|| ||

Yass-ete caturo dhammā||
saddhassa gharam esino||
saccam damo dhiti cāgo||
sa ve pecca na socati||
asmā lokā paraɱ lokaɱ||
evam pecca na socati.|| ||

Iŋgha aññe pi pucchassa||
puthu-samaṇa-brāhmaṇe||
yadi saccā damā cāgā||
khantyā bhiyyo dha vijjatī ti.|| ||

15. Kathaɱ nu dāni puccheyyaɱ||
puthu-samaṇa-brāhmaṇe||
yo haɱ ajja pajānāmi||
yo attho samparāyiko.|| ||

Atthāya vata me buddho||
vāsāyāḷavim āgato||
yo ham ajja pajānāmi||
yattha dinnam mahapphalaɱ.|| ||

So ahaɱ vicarissāmi||
gāmā gāmaɱ purā puraɱ||
namassamāno sambuddham||
dhammassa ca sudhammatan ti.|| ||

Indaka-vaggo.|| ||

Tass'uddānaɱ:|| ||

Indako Sakka-Lomo ca||
Maṇibhaddo ca Sānu ca||
Piyaŋkara-Punabbasu||
Sudatto ca dve Sukkā Cīrā Alavan ti.|| ||

Yakkha-saɱyuttam samattaɱ.|| ||

[page 216]

 

 

Book XI

Sakka Saɱyutta

Chapter I: Paṭhamo Vaggo

1. Suvira

1. Evaɱ me sutaɱ ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū amantesi|| ||

Bhikkhavo ti.|| ||

Bhadante ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

3. Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

4. Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave asurā deve abhiyaɱsu||
atha kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Suvīraɱ devaputtam āmantesi|| ||

Ete tāta Suvīra asurā deve abhiyanti||
gaccha tāta Suvīra asure paccuyyāhīti|| ||

Evam bhaddanta vā ti kho bhikkhave Suvīro devaputto Sakkassa devānam indassa paṭissutvā pamādam āpādesi.|| ||

5. Dutiyam pi kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Suvīraɱ devaputtam āmantesi||
Ete tāta Suvīra asurā deve abhiyanti||
gaccha tāta Suvīra asure paccuyyāhīti|| ||

Evam bhadanta vā ti kho bhikkhave Suvīro devaputto Sakkassa devānam indassa paṭissutvā pamādam āpādesi.|| ||

6. Tatiyam pi kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Suvīraɱ devaputtam āmantesi|| ||

Ete tāta Suvīra asurā deve abhiyanti||
gaccha tāta Suvīra asure paccuyyāhīti|| ||

Evam bhaddanta vā ti kho bhikkhave Suvīro devaputto Sakkassa devānam indassa paṭissutvā pamādam āpādesi.|| ||

[page 217]

7. Atha kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Suvīraɱ devaputtaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Anuṭṭhahaɱ avāyamaɱ||
sukhaɱ yatrādhigacchati||
Suvīra tattha gacchāhi||
māñca tattheva pāpayā ti.|| ||

8. Alasassa anuṭṭhātā||
na ca kiccāni kāraye||
sabbakāmasamiddhassa||
taɱ me Sakka varaɱ disan ti.|| ||

9. Yatthālaso anuṭṭhātā||
accantaɱ sukham edhati||
Suvīra tattha gacchāhi||
mañca tatth-eva pāpayā ti.|| ||

10. Akammanā devaseṭṭha||
Sakka vindemu yaɱ sukhaɱ||
asokam anupāyāsaɱ||
tam me Sakka varaɱ disan ti||
11. Sa ce atthi akammena||
koci kvaci na jīyati||
nibbānassa hi so maggo||
Suvīra tattha gacchāhi||
mañca tatth-eva pāpayā ti.|| ||

12. So hi nāma bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo sakam puññaphalam upajīvamāno devānaɱ Tāvatiɱsānam issariyādhipaccam rajjaɱ karonto uṭṭhāna-viriyassa vaṇṇavādī bhavissati||
idha kho taɱ bhikkhave sobhetha yaɱ tumhe evaɱ svākhyāte dhammavinaye pabbajitā samānā uṭṭhaheyyātha ghaṭeyyātha vā yameyyātha appattassa pattiyā andhigatassa adhigamāya asacchikatassa sacchikariyāyā ti.|| ||

 

 

2. Susīma

1. Sāvatthiyam viharati Jetavane.|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Bhikkhavo ti.|| ||

Bhadante ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

3. Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

4. Bhūtapubbaɱ bhikkhave asurā deve abhiyaɱsu||
atha kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Susīmaɱ devaputtaɱ āmantesi||
ete tāta Susīma asurā deve abhiyanti||
gaccha tāta Susīma asure paccuyyāhīti|| ||

Evam bhadanta vā ti kho bhikkhave Susīmo devaputto Sakassa devānam indassa paṭissutvā pamādam āpādesi.|| ||

[page 218]

5. Dutiyam pi kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Susīmam devaputtam āmantesi||
pa||
dutiyam pi pamādam āpādesi.|| ||

6. Tatiyam pi kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Susīmam devaputtam āmantesi||
pa||
tatiyam pi pamādam āpādesi.|| ||

7. Atha kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Susīmaɱ devaputtaɱ gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Anuṭṭhahaɱ avāyamaɱ||
sukhaɱ yatrādhigacchati.|| ||

Susīma tattha gacchāhi||
mañ ca tatth-eva pāpayā ti.|| ||

8. Alasassa anuṭṭhātā||
na ca kiccāni kāraye||
sabbakāmasamiddhassa||
tam me Sakka varam disan ti.|| ||

9. Yatthālaso anuṭṭhātā||
accantaɱ sukham edhati||
Susīma tattha gacchāhi||
mañca tatth-eva pāpayā ti.|| ||

10. Akammanā devaseṭṭha||
Sakka vindemu yaɱ sukhaɱ||
asokam anupāyāsaɱ||
tam me Sakka varaɱ disan ti.|| ||

11. Sa ce atthi akammena||
koci kvaci na jīyati||
nibbānassa hi so maggo||
Susīma tattha gacchāhi||
mañca tatth-eva pāpayā ti.|| ||

12. So hi nāma bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo sakam puññaphalaɱ upajīvamāno devānaɱ Tāvatiɱsānam issariyādhipaccaɱ rajjam karonto uṭṭhānaviriyassa vaṇṇavādī bhavissati.|| ||

Idha kho taɱ bhikkhave sobhetha yaɱ tumhe evaɱ svākhyāte dhammavinaye pabbajitā samānā uṭṭhaheyyātha ghaṭeyyātha vāyameyyātha appattassa pattiyā anadhigatassa adhigamāya asacchikatassa sacchikiriyāyā ti.|| ||

 

 

3. Dhajaggam

1. Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati Jetavane Anāthapiṇḍikassa ārāme.|| ||

2. Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi|| ||

Bhikkhavo ti.|| ||

Bhadante ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

3. Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

4. Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave devāsurasaŋgāmo samupabbūḷho ahosi.|| ||

5. Atha kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo deve Tāvatiɱse āmantesi|| ||

Sa ce mārisā devānam saŋgāmagatānam

[page 219]

uppajjeyya bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā mam-eva tasmiɱ samaye dhajaggam ullokeyyātha||
mamaɱhi vo dhajaggaɱ ullokayataɱ yam bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitatthaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

6. No ce me dhajaggam ullokeyyātha atha Pajāpatissa devarājassa dhajaggam ullokeyyātha.|| ||

Pajāpatissa hi vo devarājassa dhajaggam ullokayataɱ yam bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitattam vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

7. No ce Pajāpatissa devarājassa dhajaggam ullokeyyātha atha Varuṇassa devarājassa dhajaggam ullokeyyātha.|| ||

Varuṇassa hi vo devarājassa dhajaggam ullokayataɱ yaɱ bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

8. No ce Varuṇassa devarājassa dhajaggam ullokeyyātha atha §sānassa devarājassa dhajaggam ullokeyyātha.|| ||

§sānassa hi vo devarājassa dhajaggaɱ ullokayataɱ yam bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitattam vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

9. Taɱ kho pana bhikkhave Sakkassa vā devānam indassa dhajaggam ullokayatam.|| ||

Pajāpatissa vā devarājassa dhajaggam ullokayataɱ.|| ||

Varuṇassa vā devarājassa dhajaggam ullokayataɱ||
§sānassa vā devarājassa dhajaggam ullokayatam.|| ||

yaɱ bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyethā pi no pi pahīyetha.|| ||

10. Tam kissa hetu?|| ||

Sakko hi bhikkhave devānam indo avītarāgo avītadoso avītamoho bhīru chambhī utrāsī palāyī ti.|| ||

11. Ahaɱ ca kho bhikkhave evaɱ vadāmi||
sa ce tumhākam bhikkhave araññagatānam vā rukkhamūlagatānaɱ vā suññāgāragatānam vā uppajjeyya bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā mam eva tasmiɱ samaye anussareyyātha.|| ||

Iti pi so Bhagavā arahaɱ sammāsambuddho vijjācaraṇasampanno sugato lokavidū anuttaro purisadammasārathi satthā devamanussānam buddho bhagavā ti.|| ||

12. Mamaɱ hi vo bhikkhave anussarataɱ yam bhavissati bhayam vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

[page 220]

13. No ce mam anussareyyātha atha dhammam anussareyyātha.|| ||

Svākhyāto Bhagavatā dhammo sandiṭṭhiko akāliko ehipassiko opanayiko paccattaɱ veditabbo viññūhī ti.|| ||

14. Dhammaɱ hi vo bhikkhave anussarataɱ yam bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

15. No ce dhammam anussareyyātha atha saŋgham anussareyyātha|| ||

Supaṭipaṇṇo Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ujupaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
ñāyapaṭipanno Bhagavato sāvaka-saŋgho||
sāmīcipaṭipaṇṇo Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho yad idam cattāri purisayugāni aṭṭha purisa-puggalā esa Bhagavato sāvakasaŋgho āhuneyyo pāhuneyyo dakkhiṇeyyo añjalikaraṇīyo anuttaram puññakkhettam lokassā ti.|| ||

16. Saŋghaɱ hi vo bhikkhave anussarataɱ yam bhavissati bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā lomahaɱso vā so pahīyissati.|| ||

17. Taɱ kissa hetu|| ||

Tathāgato hi bhikkhave arahaɱ sammāsambuddho vītarāgo vītadoso vītamoho abhīru acchambhī anutrāsī apalāyī ti.|| ||

18. Idam avoca Bhagavā||
idaɱ vatvāna Sugato athāparam etad avoca satthā.|| ||

Araññe rukkhamūle vā||
suññāgāre vā bhikkhavo||
anussaretha sambuddhaɱ||
bhayaɱ tumhākaɱ no siyā.|| ||

No ce buddhaɱ sareyyātha||
lokajeṭṭham narāsabhaɱ||
atha dhammaɱ sareyyātha||
niyyānikaɱ sudesitaɱ.|| ||

No ce dhammaɱ sareyyātha||
niyyānikaɱ sudesitaɱ||
atha saŋghaɱ sareyyātha||
puññakkhettam anuttaraɱ.|| ||

Evam buddham sarantānaɱ||
dhammaɱ saŋghañ ca bhikkhavo||
bhayaɱ vā chambhitattaɱ vā||
lomahaɱso na hessatī ti.|| ||

 

 

4. Vepacitti (or Khanti)

1. Sāvatthiyam Jetavane||
pa||
2. Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

[page 221]

3. Bhūtapubbaɱ bhikkhave devāsurasaŋgāmo samupabbūḷho ahosi||
4. Atha kho bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo asure āmantesi|| ||

Sace mārisā devānam asurasaŋgāme samupabbūḷhe asurā jineyyuɱ devā parājeyyuɱ||
yena naɱ Sakkam devānam indaɱ kaṇṭhe pañcamehi bandhanehi bandhitvā mama santike āneyyātha asurapuran ti.|| ||

5. Sakko pi kho bhikkhave devānam indo deve Tāvatiɱse āmantesi|| ||

Sace mārisā devānam asurasaŋgāme samupabbūḷhe devā jineyyuɱ asurā parājeyyuɱ||
yena naɱ Vepacittim asurindaɱ kaṇṭhe pañcamehi bandhanehi bandhitvā mama santike āneyyātha Sudhammam sabbhan ti.|| ||

6. Tasmiɱ kho pana bhikkhave saŋgāme devā jiniɱsu asurā parājiɱsu.|| ||

7. Atha kho bhikkhave devā Tavatiɱsā Vepacittim asurindam kaṇṭhe pañcamehi bandhanehi bandhitvā Sakassa devānam indassa santike ānesum Sudhammaɱ sabhaɱ.|| ||

8. Tatra sudaɱ bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo kaṇṭhe pañcamehi bandhanehi baddho Sakkam devānam indaɱ Sudhammam sabham pavisantañ ca nikkhamantañ ca asabbhāhi pharusāhi vācāhi akkosati paribhāsati.|| ||

9. Atha kho bhikkhave Mātali-saŋgāhako Sakkaɱ devānam indam gāthāya ajjhabhāsi:|| ||

Bhayā nu mathavā Sakka||
dubbalyā no titikkhasi||
suṇanto pharusam vācaɱ||
sammukhā Vepacittino ti.|| ||

10. Nāham bhayā na dubbalyā||
khamāmi Vepacittino||
kathaɱ hi mādiso viññū||
bālena paṭisaɱyuje ti.|| ||

11. Bhiyyo bālā pakujjheyyuɱ||
no c-assa paṭisedhako||
tasmā bhusena daṇḍena||
dhīro bālaɱ nisedhaye ti.|| ||

12. Etad eva ahaɱ maññe||
bālassa paṭisedhanaɱ||
paraɱ saŋkupitam ñatvā||
yo sato upasammatī ti.|| ||

13. Etad eva titikkhāya||
vajjam passāmi Vāsava||
yadā naɱ maññati bālo||
bhayā myāyam titikkhati||
ajjhārūhati dummedho||
go va bhiyyo palāyinan ti.|| ||

[page 222]

14. Kāmam maññatu vā mā vā||
bhayā myāyaɱ titikkhati||
sadatthaparamā atthā||
khantyā bhiyyo na vijjati.|| ||

yo have balavā santo||
dubbalassa titikkhati||
tam āhu paramaɱ khantiɱ||
niccam khamati dubbalo.|| ||

Abalan-tam balam āhu||
yassa bālabalam balaɱ.|| ||

Balassa dhammaguttassa||
paṭivattā na vijjati.|| ||

Tass'eva tena pāpiyo||
yo kuddhaɱ paṭikujjhati||
kuddham apaṭikujjhanto||
saŋgāmam jeti dujjayaɱ.|| ||

Ubhinnam atthaɱ carati||
attano ca parassa ca||
paraɱ saŋkupitaɱ ñatvā||
yo sato upasammati.|| ||

Ubhinnam tikicchantaɱ taɱ||
attano ca parassa ca||
janā maññanti bālo ti||
ye dhammassa akovidā ti.|| ||

15. So hi nāma bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo sakaɱ puññaphalam upajīvamāno devānaɱ Tāvatiɱsānaɱ issariyadhipaccaɱ rajjaɱ karonto khantisoraccassa vaṇṇavādī bhavissati.|| ||

16. Idha kho taɱ bhikkhave sobhetha yaɱ tumhe evaɱ svākhyāte dhammavinaye pabbajitā samānā khamā ca bhaveyyātha soratā cā ti.|| ||

 

 

5. Subhāsitaɱ-jayaɱ

1. Sāvatthi nidānaɱ.|| ||

2. Bhūtapubbam bhikkhave devāsurasaŋgāmo samupabbūḷho ahosi.|| ||

3. Atha kho bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo Sakkaɱ devānam indam etad avoca:|| ||

Hotu devānam inda subhāsitena jayo ti.|| ||

Hotu Vepacitti subhāsitena jayo ti.|| ||

4. Atha kho bhikkhave devā ca asurā ca pārisajje ṭhapesuɱ||
ime no subhāsitaɱ dubbhāsitam ājānissantī ti.|| ||

5. Atha kho bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo Sakkaɱ devānam indam etad avoca:|| ||

Bhaṇa devānam inda gāthan ti.|| ||

6. Evaɱ vutte bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Vepacittim asurindam etad avoca:|| ||

Tumhe khv-attha Vepacitti pubbadevā||
bhaṇa Vepacitti gāthan ti.|| ||

[page 223]

7. Evaɱ vutte bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Bhiyyo bālā pakujjheyyuɱ||
no c-assa paṭisedhako||
tasmā bhusena daṇḍena||
dhīro bālam nisedhaye ti.|| ||

8. Bhāsitāya kho pana bhikkhave Vepacittinā asurindena gāthāya asurā anumodiɱsu||
devā tuṇhī ahesuɱ.|| ||

9. Atha kho bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo Sakkaɱ devānam indam etad avoca:|| ||

Bhaṇa devānam inda gāthan ti.|| ||

10. Evam vutte bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo imaɱ gātham abhāsi:|| ||

Etad eva ahaɱ maññe||
bālassa paṭisedhanaɱ||
paraɱ saŋkupitaɱ ñatvā||
yo sato upasammatī ti.|| ||

11. Bhāsitāya kho pana bhikkhave Sakkena devānam indena gāthāya devā anumodiɱsu||
asurā tuṇhī ahesuɱ.|| ||

12. Atha kho bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo Vepacittim asurindam etad avoca:|| ||

Bhaṇa Vepacitti gāthan ti.|| ||

Etad eva titikkhāya||
vajjaɱ passāmi Vāsava||
yadā naɱ maññati bālo||
bhayā myāyaɱ titikkhati||
ajjhārūhati dummedho||
go va bhiyyo palāyinan ti.|| ||

13. Bhāsitāya kho pana bhikkhave Vepacittinā asurindena gāthāya asurā anumodiɱsu||
devā tuṇhī ahesuɱ.|| ||

14. Atha kho bhikkhave Vepacitti asurindo Sakkaɱ devā. nam indam etad avoca:|| ||

Bhaṇa devānam inda gāthan ti.|| ||

15. Evaɱ vutte bhikkhave Sakko devānam indo imā gāthāyo abhāsi:|| ||

Kāmaɱ maññatu vā mā vā||
bhayā myāyam titikkhati||
sadatthaparamā atthā||
khantyā bhiyyo na vijjati.|| ||

Yo have balavā santo||
dubbalassa titikkhati||
tam āhu paramaɱ khantiɱ||
niccaɱ khamati dubbalo||
Abalan-tam balaɱ āhu||
yassa bālabalaɱ balaɱ||
balassa dhammaguttassa||
paṭivattā na vijjati.|| ||

Tass'eva tena pāpiyo||
yo kuddhaɱ paṭikujjhati||
kuddham appaṭikujjhanto||
saŋgāmaɱ jeti dujjayaɱ.|| ||

Ubhinnam atthaɱ carati||
attano ca parassa ca||
paraɱ saŋkupitaɱ ñatvā||
yo sato upasammati.|| ||

[page 224]

Ubhinnam tikicchantaɱ taɱ||
attano ca parassa ca||
janā maññanti bālo ti||
ye dhammassa akovidā ti.|| ||

16. Bhāsitāsu kho pana bhikkhave Sakkena devānam indena gāthāsu devā anumodiɱsu||
asurā tuṇhī ahesuɱ.|| ||

17. Atha kho bhikkhave devānañ ca asurānañ ca parisajjā etad avocuɱ:|| ||

18. Bhāsitā kho Vepacittinā asurindena gāthayo||
tā ca kho sadaṇḍāvacarā satthāvacarā iti bhaṇḍanam iti viggaho iti kalaho ti.|| ||
